1. /**
2.  * @fileoverview SpellsProvider — seeds spells from 5etools PHB data.
3.  *
4.  * Reads: src/lib/5etools-data/spells-phb.json
5.  * Creates: Spell documents via spells-service
6.  *
7.  * Flow per item:
8.  *  1. Map deterministic fields (school, circle, components, castingTime, dice, etc.)
9.  *  2. Call this.translateItem(name, description) defined in BaseProvider
10.  *  3. Check if spell with that name already exists
11.  *  4. If not, create it
12.  */
13. 
14. import mongoose from 'mongoose';
15. import { BaseProvider, convertFeetToMeters } from '../base-provider';
16. import type { CreateSpellInput } from '../../../src/features/spells/types/spells.types';
17. import { createSpell } from '../../../src/features/spells/api/spells-service';
18. import { Spell } from '../../../src/features/spells/models/spell';
19. import dbConnect from '../../../src/core/database/db';
20. 
21. // ─── 5etools input types ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────
22. 
23. interface FiveEToolsTime {
24.     number: number;
25.     unit: string;
26.     condition?: string;
27. }
28. 
29. interface FiveEToolsRange {
30.     type: string;
31.     distance?: {
32.         type: string;
33.         amount?: number;
34.     };
35. }
36. 
37. interface FiveEToolsComponents {
38.     v?: boolean;
39.     s?: boolean;
40.     m?: boolean | string;
41. }
42. 
43. interface FiveEToolsDuration {
44.     type: string;
45.     concentration?: boolean;
46.     duration?: {
47.         type: string;
48.         amount?: number;
49.     };
50. }
51. 
52. interface FiveEToolsEntriesHigherLevel {
53.     type: string;
54.     name: string;
55.     entries: string[];
56. }
57. 
58. export interface FiveEToolsSpell {
59.     name: string;
60.     source: string;
61.     page?: number;
62.     level: number;
63.     school: string;
64.     time: FiveEToolsTime[];
65.     range: FiveEToolsRange;
66.     components: FiveEToolsComponents;
67.     duration: FiveEToolsDuration[];
68.     entries: (string | Record<string, unknown>)[];
69.     entriesHigherLevel?: FiveEToolsEntriesHigherLevel[];
70.     savingThrow?: string[];
71.     meta?: { ritual?: boolean };
72.     damageInflict?: string[];
73.     scalingLevelDice?: unknown;
74. }
75. 
76. // ─── Mapping tables ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
77. 
78. const SCHOOL_MAP: Record<string, CreateSpellInput['school']> = {
79.     A: 'Abjuração',
80.     C: 'Conjuração',
81.     D: 'Adivinhação',
82.     E: 'Encantamento',
83.     V: 'Evocação',
84.     I: 'Ilusão',
85.     N: 'Necromancia',
86.     T: 'Transmutação',
87. };
88. 
89. const SAVE_ATTRIBUTE_MAP: Record<string, NonNullable<CreateSpellInput['saveAttribute']>> = {
90.     strength: 'Força',
91.     dexterity: 'Destreza',
92.     constitution: 'Constituição',
93.     intelligence: 'Inteligência',
94.     wisdom: 'Sabedoria',
95.     charisma: 'Carisma',
96. };
97. 
98. const DURATION_TYPE_LABELS: Record<string, string> = {
99.     round: 'rodada',
100.     rounds: 'rodadas',
101.     minute: 'minuto',
102.     minutes: 'minutos',
103.     hour: 'hora',
104.     hours: 'horas',
105.     day: 'dia',
106.     days: 'dias',
107. };
108. 
109. // ─── Helpers ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
110. 
111. /** D&D standard: 5 ft = 1.5 m → multiply by 0.3 */
112. function feetToMeters(feet: number): string {
113.     const m = feet * 0.3;
114.     return Number.isInteger(m) ? String(m) : m.toFixed(1).replace('.', ',');
115. }
116. 
117. /** 1 mile = 1.5 km (consistent with 5 ft = 1.5 m) */
118. function milesToKm(miles: number): string {
119.     const km = miles * 1.5;
120.     return Number.isInteger(km) ? String(km) : km.toFixed(1).replace('.', ',');
121. }
122. 
123. const DICE_REGEX = /\{@(?:damage|hit)\s+(\d+)d(\d+)(?:[^}]*)?\}/;
124. const SCALE_DICE_REGEX = /\{@scaledamage\s+[^|]*\|[^|]*\|(\d+)d(\d+)\}/;
125. const VALID_DICE = ['d4', 'd6', 'd8', 'd10', 'd12', 'd20'];
126. 
127. function extractBaseDice(entries: (string | Record<string, unknown>)[]): CreateSpellInput['baseDice'] {
128.     for (const entry of entries) {
129.         if (typeof entry !== 'string') continue;
130.         const match = entry.match(DICE_REGEX);
131.         if (match && VALID_DICE.includes(`d${match[2]}`)) {
132.             return {
133.                 quantidade: parseInt(match[1], 10),
134.                 tipo: `d${match[2]}` as NonNullable<CreateSpellInput['baseDice']>['tipo'],
135.             };
136.         }
137.     }
138.     return undefined;
139. }
140. 
141. function extractExtraDicePerLevel(
142.     entries: (string | Record<string, unknown>)[],
143.     higherLevel?: FiveEToolsEntriesHigherLevel[],
144. ): CreateSpellInput['extraDicePerLevel'] {
145.     const allEntries = [
146.         ...entries.filter((e): e is string => typeof e === 'string'),
147.         ...(higherLevel?.flatMap((h) => h.entries) ?? []),
148.     ];
149.     for (const entry of allEntries) {
150.         const match = entry.match(SCALE_DICE_REGEX);
151.         if (match && VALID_DICE.includes(`d${match[2]}`)) {
152.             return {
153.                 quantidade: parseInt(match[1], 10),
154.                 tipo: `d${match[2]}` as NonNullable<CreateSpellInput['extraDicePerLevel']>['tipo'],
155.             };
156.         }
157.     }
158.     return undefined;
159. }
160. 
161. function mapCastingTime(spell: FiveEToolsSpell): CreateSpellInput['castingTime'] {
162.     if (spell.meta?.ritual) return 'Ritual';
163.     switch (spell.time[0]?.unit) {
164.         case 'action':   return 'Ação';
165.         case 'bonus':    return 'Ação Bônus';
166.         case 'reaction': return 'Reação';
167.         default:         return undefined;
168.     }
169. }
170. 
171. function mapComponents(spell: FiveEToolsSpell): CreateSpellInput['component'] {
172.     const comps: CreateSpellInput['component'] = [];
173.     if (spell.components.v) comps.push('Verbal');
174.     if (spell.components.s) comps.push('Somático');
175.     if (spell.components.m) comps.push('Material');
176.     if (spell.duration.some((d) => d.concentration === true)) comps.push('Concentração');
177.     return comps;
178. }
179. 
180. function mapRange(range: FiveEToolsRange): string | undefined {
181.     if (range.type === 'self')      return 'Pessoal';
182.     if (range.type === 'touch')     return 'Toque';
183.     if (range.type === 'sight')     return 'Linha de visão';
184.     if (range.type === 'unlimited') return 'Ilimitado';
185.     if (range.distance?.amount !== undefined) {
186.         const { type, amount } = range.distance;
187.         if (type === 'feet')  return `${feetToMeters(amount)} metros`;
188.         if (type === 'miles') return `${milesToKm(amount)} km`;
189.         return `${amount} ${type}`;
190.     }
191.     return undefined;
192. }
193. 
194. function mapDuration(durations: FiveEToolsDuration[]): string | undefined {
195.     if (!durations.length) return undefined;
196.     const d = durations[0];
197.     if (d.type === 'instant')   return 'Instantâneo';
198.     if (d.type === 'permanent') return 'Permanente';
199.     if (d.type === 'special')   return 'Especial';
200.     if (d.type === 'timed' && d.duration) {
201.         const amount = d.duration.amount ?? 1;
202.         const unit = DURATION_TYPE_LABELS[d.duration.type] ?? d.duration.type;
203.         const prefix = d.concentration ? 'Concentração, até ' : '';
204.         return `${prefix}${amount} ${amount === 1 ? unit : unit + 's'}`.replace(/ss$/, 's');
205.     }
206.     return undefined;
207. }
208. 
209. /** Strip 5etools inline tag syntax from entry text before sending to AI. */
210. function cleanEntryText(text: string): string {
211.     return text
212.         .replace(/\{@damage\s+([^}]+)\}/g, '$1')
213.         .replace(/\{@scaledamage\s+([^|]+)\|[^|]+\|([^}]+)\}/g, '$2')
214.         .replace(/\{@dice\s+([^}]+)\}/g, '$1')
215.         .replace(/\{@hit\s+([^}]+)\}/g, '+$1')
216.         .replace(/\{@dc\s+([^}]+)\}/g, 'DC $1')
217.         .replace(/\{@[a-z]+\s+([^}|]+)(?:\|[^}]*)?\}/gi, '$1')
218.         .trim();
219. }
220. 
221. /** Build an HTML description in English from the spell entries, ready for translation. */
222. function buildEntriesHtml(spell: FiveEToolsSpell): string {
223.     const parts: string[] = [];
224. 
225.     for (const entry of spell.entries) {
226.         if (typeof entry === 'string') {
227.             parts.push(`<p>${cleanEntryText(entry)}</p>`);
228.         } else if (typeof entry === 'object' && entry !== null) {
229.             const e = entry as { type?: string; name?: string; entries?: string[] };
230.             if (e.entries) {
231.                 const texts = e.entries
232.                     .filter((s): s is string => typeof s === 'string')
233.                     .map(cleanEntryText);
234.                 if (e.name) {
235.                     parts.push(`<p><strong>${e.name}.</strong> ${texts.join(' ')}</p>`);
236.                 } else {
237.                     texts.forEach((t) => parts.push(`<p>${t}</p>`));
238.                 }
239.             }
240.         }
241.     }
242. 
243.     if (spell.entriesHigherLevel) {
244.         for (const section of spell.entriesHigherLevel) {
245.             const text = section.entries.map(cleanEntryText).join(' ');
246.             parts.push(`<p><strong>At Higher Levels.</strong> ${text}</p>`);
247.         }
248.     }
249. 
250.     return parts.join('');
251. }
252. 
253. // ─── SpellsProvider ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
254. 
255. export class SpellsProvider extends BaseProvider<FiveEToolsSpell, CreateSpellInput> {
256.     readonly name = 'Spells';
257.     readonly dataFilePath = 'src/lib/5etools-data/spells-phb.json';
258.     readonly dataKey = 'spell';
259. 
260.     async processItem(spell: FiveEToolsSpell): Promise<CreateSpellInput | null> {
261.         const school = SCHOOL_MAP[spell.school];
262.         if (!school) {
263.             this.log(`Unknown school code "${spell.school}" for spell "${spell.name}" — skipping`, 'warn');
264.             return null;
265.         }
266. 
267.         // Translate name + description via the configured translator
268.         const entriesHtml = buildEntriesHtml(spell);
269.         const { name, description } = await this.translateItem(spell.name, entriesHtml);
270. 
271.         // Deterministic field mapping (no AI needed)
272.         return {
273.             name,
274.             description,
275.             circle: spell.level,
276.             school,
277.             castingTime: mapCastingTime(spell),
278.             component: mapComponents(spell),
279.             range: mapRange(spell.range),
280.             duration: mapDuration(spell.duration),
281.             saveAttribute: spell.savingThrow?.[0]
282.                 ? SAVE_ATTRIBUTE_MAP[spell.savingThrow[0]]
283.                 : undefined,
284.             baseDice: extractBaseDice(spell.entries),
285.             extraDicePerLevel: extractExtraDicePerLevel(spell.entries, spell.entriesHigherLevel),
286.             source: spell.page ? `LDJ pág. ${spell.page}` : 'LDJ',
287.             status: 'active',
288.         };
289.     }
290. 
291.     async findExisting(spell: CreateSpellInput): Promise<CreateSpellInput | null> {
292.         await dbConnect();
293.         const doc = await Spell.findOne({ name: spell.name }).lean();
294.         if (!doc) return null;
295.         return {
296.             name: doc.name,
297.             description: doc.description,
298.             circle: doc.circle,
299.             school: doc.school,
300.             castingTime: doc.castingTime,
301.             component: doc.component,
302.             range: doc.range ?? undefined,
303.             area: doc.area ?? undefined,
304.             duration: doc.duration ?? undefined,
305.             saveAttribute: doc.saveAttribute ?? undefined,
306.             baseDice: doc.baseDice ?? undefined,
307.             additionalBaseDice: doc.additionalBaseDice ?? undefined,
308.             extraDicePerLevel: doc.extraDicePerLevel ?? undefined,
309.             additionalExtraDicePerLevel: doc.additionalExtraDicePerLevel ?? undefined,
310.             image: doc.image ?? undefined,
311.             source: doc.source ?? undefined,
312.             status: doc.status,
313.         };
314.     }
315. 
316.     async update(spell: CreateSpellInput): Promise<void> {
317.         await dbConnect();
318.         await Spell.findOneAndUpdate(
319.             { name: spell.name },
320.             { $set: spell },
321.             { runValidators: true },
322.         );
323.     }
324. 
325.     async create(spell: CreateSpellInput): Promise<void> {
326.         await createSpell(spell, 'seed-script');
327.     }
328. 
329.     override getItemLabel(item: CreateSpellInput): string {
330.         return item.name;
331.     }
332. }
333.
```

</details>

```
1. /**
2.  * @fileoverview Abstract base class for all seed data providers.
3.  *
4.  * Each provider reads a 5etools JSON file, translates items via a pluggable
5.  * translator, checks for duplicates, and creates records in the system.
6.  *
7.  * Usage:
8.  *   class MyProvider extends BaseProvider<TInput, TOutput> { ... }
9.  *
10.  * ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
11.  * IMAGENS DO 5ETOOLS
12.  * ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
13.  * Os JSONs do 5etools NÃO contêm URLs de imagem diretamente. Em vez disso,
14.  * usam a flag booleana `hasFluffImages: true` para indicar que existe imagem
15.  * disponível externamente.
16.  *
17.  * Para exibir a imagem na UI, buscar via:
18.  *   https://5e.tools/img/{source}/{name}.webp
19.  *   (ex: https://5e.tools/img/MPMM/Aarakocra.webp)
20.  *
21.  * Cobertura por tipo de entidade:
22.  *   - Classes  : ~93% têm imagem (14 de 15 classes)
23.  *   - Raças    : ~84% têm imagem (133 de 158 raças)
24.  *   - Itens    : ~31% têm imagem (764 de 2451 itens)
25.  *   - Base items: ~28% têm imagem (55 de 196 itens)
26.  *   - Feats    : ~11% têm imagem (29 de 265 feats)
27.  *   - Spells   : ~3%  têm imagem (12 de 361 spells)
28.  *
29.  * Ao implementar, verificar `hasFluffImages === true` antes de tentar
30.  * carregar a imagem para evitar requisições desnecessárias.
31.  * ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
32.  */
33. 
34. import fs from 'fs';
35. import path from 'path';
36. import terminal from 'terminal-kit';
37. import type { BaseTranslator } from './translation/base-translator';
38. import {
39.     loadAllEntries,
40.     saveEntries,
41.     applyGlossary,
42.     parseGlossaryInput,
43.     type GlossaryEntry,
44. } from './glossary/glossary-store';
45. import {
46.     readProgress as dbReadProgress,
47.     saveProgress as dbSaveProgress,
48. } from './progress/progress-store';
49. 
50. const term = terminal.terminal;
51. 
52. export type LogLevel = 'info' | 'success' | 'error' | 'warn' | 'dim';
53. 
54. export interface DiffEntry {
55.     field: string;
56.     oldValue: unknown;
57.     newValue: unknown;
58. }
59. 
60. function formatValue(v: unknown): string {
61.     if (v === undefined) return '(não definido)';
62.     if (v === null) return '(nulo)';
63.     if (typeof v === 'string') return v;
64.     return JSON.stringify(v);
65. }
66. 
67. function truncateStr(s: string, maxLen = 120): string {
68.     return s.length > maxLen ? s.slice(0, maxLen - 3) + '...' : s;
69. }
70. 
71. // ─── Colored JSON printer ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────
72. 
73. /**
74.  * Prints a syntax-highlighted JSON representation of `obj` to the terminal.
75.  *
76.  * Color scheme:
77.  *   - Keys        → yellow
78.  *   - Strings     → green
79.  *   - Numbers     → cyan
80.  *   - Booleans    → blue
81.  *   - null        → gray
82.  *   - Brackets    → bold white
83.  *   - Punctuation → default
84.  */
85. function printColoredJson(obj: unknown): void {
86.     const str = JSON.stringify(obj, null, 2);
87.     // Tokenize: quoted strings (optionally followed by ": "), numbers,
88.     // keywords, brackets, punctuation, and whitespace.
89.     const re = /("(?:[^"\\]|\\.)*")(\s*:)?|true|false|null|-?\d+(?:\.\d+)?(?:[eE][+-]?\d+)?|[{}\[\],:]|\n|[^\S\n]+/g;
90. 
91.     let m: RegExpExecArray | null;
92.     while ((m = re.exec(str)) !== null) {
93.         const tok = m[0];
94.         const quotedStr = m[1];
95.         const colonSuffix = m[2];
96. 
97.         if (quotedStr !== undefined) {
98.             if (colonSuffix !== undefined) {
99.                 term.yellow(quotedStr);
100.                 term(colonSuffix);
```

```
100.                 term(colonSuffix);
101.             } else {
102.                 term.cyan(quotedStr);
103.             }
104.         } else if (tok === 'true' || tok === 'false') {
105.             term.blue(tok);
106.         } else if (tok === 'null') {
107.             term.gray(tok);
108.         } else if (tok === '{' || tok === '}' || tok === '[' || tok === ']') {
109.             term.bold.white(tok);
110.         } else if (/^-?\d/.test(tok)) {
111.             term.green(tok);
112.         } else {
113.             term(tok);
114.         }
115.     }
116. }
117. 
118. const PROJECT_ROOT = path.resolve(__dirname, '../../');
119. 
120. // ─── Unit conversion ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
121. 
122. /**
123.  * Converts any "X pés", "X feet", "X foot" or "X ft" occurrences in a text
124.  * to meters using the D&D standard (5 ft = 1.5 m, i.e. × 0.3).
125.  * Also converts "X mile(s)" to km (1 mile = 1.5 km by the same standard).
126.  */
127. export function convertFeetToMeters(text: string): string {
128.     return text
129.         .replace(/(\d+(?:[.,]\d+)?)\s*(?:pés?|feet|foot|ft\.?)/gi, (_, numStr: string) => {
130.             const feet = parseFloat(numStr.replace(',', '.'));
131.             const meters = feet * 0.3;
132.             const formatted = Number.isInteger(meters)
133.                 ? String(meters)
134.                 : meters.toFixed(1).replace('.', ',');
135.             return `${formatted} metros`;
136.         })
137.         .replace(/(\d+(?:[.,]\d+)?)\s*(?:milhas?|miles?)/gi, (_, numStr: string) => {
138.             const miles = parseFloat(numStr.replace(',', '.'));
139.             const km = miles * 1.5;
140.             const formatted = Number.isInteger(km)
141.                 ? String(km)
142.                 : km.toFixed(1).replace('.', ',');
143.             return `${formatted} km`;
144.         });
145. }
146. 
147. // ─── Base class ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
148. 
149. export abstract class BaseProvider<TInput, TOutput> {
150.     abstract readonly name: string;
151.     abstract readonly dataFilePath: string;
152.     abstract readonly dataKey: string;
153. 
154.     private progressBar: terminal.Terminal.ProgressBarController | null = null;
155.     private currentTotal = 0;
156.     private testMode = false;
157.     private autoMode = false;
158. 
159.     // ─── Translator ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
160. 
161.     private translator: BaseTranslator | null = null;
162. 
163.     setTranslator(translator: BaseTranslator): void {
164.         this.translator = translator;
165.     }
166. 
167.     setTestMode(enabled: boolean): void {
168.         this.testMode = enabled;
169.     }
170. 
171.     setAutoMode(enabled: boolean): void {
172.         this.autoMode = enabled;
173.     }
174. 
175.     /**
176.      * Translates a D&D item name and pre-built HTML description from English
177.      * to Brazilian Portuguese via the configured translator.
178.      */
179.     async translateItem(
180.         name: string,
181.         descriptionHtml: string,
182.     ): Promise<{ name: string; description: string }> {
183.         if (!this.translator) {
184.             throw new Error('No translator configured. Call setTranslator() before running.');
185.         }
186.         return this.translator.translateItem(name, descriptionHtml);
187.     }
188. 
189.     readDataFile(): TInput[] {
190.         const fullPath = path.resolve(PROJECT_ROOT, this.dataFilePath);
191.         const raw = fs.readFileSync(fullPath, 'utf-8');
192.         const parsed = JSON.parse(raw);
193.         const items = parsed[this.dataKey];
194.         if (!Array.isArray(items)) {
195.             throw new Error(`Key "${this.dataKey}" not found or not an array in ${fullPath}`);
196.         }
197.         return items as TInput[];
198.     }
199. 
200.     // ─── Progress tracking ────────────────────────────────────────────────────
201. 
202.     async readProgress(): Promise<number> {
203.         return dbReadProgress(this.name);
204.     }
205. 
206.     async saveProgress(index: number): Promise<void> {
207.         await dbSaveProgress(this.name, index);
208.     }
209. 
210.     // ─── Terminal UI ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
211. 
212.     log(message: string, level: LogLevel = 'info'): void {
213.         switch (level) {
214.             case 'success':
215.                 term.green(`✓ ${message}\n`);
216.                 break;
217.             case 'error':
218.                 term.red(`✗ ${message}\n`);
219.                 break;
220.             case 'warn':
221.                 term.yellow(`⚠ ${message}\n`);
222.                 break;
223.             case 'dim':
224.                 term.gray(`  ${message}\n`);
225.                 break;
226.             case 'info':
227.             default:
228.                 term.cyan(`ℹ ${message}\n`);
229.                 break;
230.         }
231.     }
232. 
233.     initProgressBar(total: number, startIndex: number): void {
234.         this.currentTotal = total;
235.         term('\n');
236.         this.progressBar = term.progressBar({
237.             width: 60,
238.             title: `${this.name}:`,
239.             eta: true,
240.             percent: true,
241.             items: total,
242.         });
243.         if (startIndex > 0) {
244.             this.progressBar.update({ progress: startIndex / total });
245.         }
246.     }
247. 
248.     updateProgressBar(current: number, itemName: string): void {
249.         if (!this.progressBar) return;
250.         this.progressBar.update({
251.             progress: current / this.currentTotal,
252.             title: `${this.name} [${current}/${this.currentTotal}] ${itemName}`,
253.         });
254.     }
255. 
256.     stopProgressBar(): void {
257.         if (this.progressBar) {
258.             this.progressBar.stop();
259.             this.progressBar = null;
260.         }
261.     }
262. 
263.     // ─── Diff helpers ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
264. 
265.     /**
266.      * Normalizes a value before diff comparison.
267.      * Empty arrays, empty strings, and null are treated as equivalent to
268.      * undefined because the DB may return null/""/[] for unset fields while
269.      * incoming data uses undefined, and semantically they mean "not set".
270.      */
271.     private normalizeForDiff(v: unknown): unknown {
272.         if (v === null) return undefined;
273.         if (v === '') return undefined;
274.         if (Array.isArray(v) && v.length === 0) return undefined;
275.         return v;
276.     }
277. 
278.     private diffObjects(existing: TOutput, incoming: TOutput): DiffEntry[] {
279.         const a = existing as Record<string, unknown>;
280.         const b = incoming as Record<string, unknown>;
281.         const allFields = new Set([...Object.keys(a), ...Object.keys(b)]);
282.         const diffs: DiffEntry[] = [];
283.         for (const field of allFields) {
284.             const normA = this.normalizeForDiff(a[field]);
285.             const normB = this.normalizeForDiff(b[field]);
286.             if (JSON.stringify(normA) !== JSON.stringify(normB)) {
287.                 diffs.push({ field, oldValue: a[field], newValue: b[field] });
288.             }
289.         }
290.         return diffs;
291.     }
292. 
293.     /**
294.      * Shows each conflicting field individually and lets the user decide
295.      * field by field whether to keep the existing value (←) or use the
296.      * incoming one (→). Works identically in dry-run and live mode.
297.      *
298.      * @returns A merged TOutput built from existing + chosen incoming fields.
299.      */
300.     private async resolveConflictsFieldByField(
```

</details>

300.     private async resolveConflictsFieldByField(
301.         existing: TOutput,
302.         incoming: TOutput,
303.         diffs: DiffEntry[],
304.     ): Promise<TOutput> {
305.         const label = this.getItemLabel(incoming);
306.         term('\n');
307.         term.bold(`─── Conflito: ${label} ─────────────────────────────────────────\n`);
308.         term.yellow(`  ${diffs.length} campo(s) diferente(s) — resolva cada um:\n\n`);
309. 
310.         const result = { ...(existing as Record<string, unknown>) };
311. 
312.         for (const diff of diffs) {
313.             term.bold(`  ${diff.field}:\n`);
314.             term.red(`    ← ${truncateStr(formatValue(diff.oldValue))}  (existente)\n`);
315.             term.green(`    → ${truncateStr(formatValue(diff.newValue))}  (novo)\n`);
316.             term.bold('  ← seta esquerda: manter existente  |  → seta direita: usar novo\n');
317. 
318.             const choice = await new Promise<'keep' | 'update'>((resolve) => {
319.                 term.grabInput(true);
320.                 const handler = (name: string) => {
321.                     if (name === 'CTRL_C') { term.grabInput(false); process.exit(0); }
322.                     if (name === 'LEFT') {
323.                         term.grabInput(false);
324.                         term.removeListener('key', handler);
325.                         term.yellow('  ← Mantendo existente.\n\n');
326.                         resolve('keep');
327.                     } else if (name === 'RIGHT') {
328.                         term.grabInput(false);
329.                         term.removeListener('key', handler);
330.                         term.green('  → Usando novo.\n\n');
331.                         resolve('update');
332.                     }
333.                 };
334.                 term.on('key', handler);
335.             });
336. 
337.             if (choice === 'update') {
338.                 result[diff.field] = diff.newValue;
339.             }
340.         }
341. 
342.         return result as TOutput;
343.     }
344. 
345. 
346. 
347.     /**
348.      * Applies the current glossary to all string fields of an output object.
349.      * Only processes `name` and `description` fields (both are translatable text).
350.      */
351.     private applyGlossaryToOutput(output: TOutput, entries: GlossaryEntry[]): TOutput {
352.         if (!entries.length) return output;
353.         const obj = output as Record<string, unknown>;
354.         const result = { ...obj };
355. 
356.         if (typeof result['name'] === 'string') {
357.             result['name'] = applyGlossary(entries, result['name']);
358.         }
359.         if (typeof result['description'] === 'string') {
360.             result['description'] = applyGlossary(entries, result['description']);
361.         }
362. 
363.         return result as TOutput;
364.     }
365. 
366.     // ─── Interactive review ───────────────────────────────────────────────────
367. 
368.     /**
369.      * Shows the current item and prompts the user for glossary corrections.
370.      * Loops until the user presses Enter with no input.
371.      *
372.      * @param output - The translated item to review
373.      * @param isDryRun - If true, will not save to database
374.      * @returns The final (possibly corrected) output
375.      */
376.     private async reviewAndConfirmItem(
377.         output: TOutput,
378.         isDryRun: boolean,
379.     ): Promise<TOutput> {
380.         let entries = await loadAllEntries();
381.         let current = this.applyGlossaryToOutput(output, entries);
382. 
383.         // eslint-disable-next-line no-constant-condition
384.         while (true) {
385.             // Display current state
386.             term('\n');
387.             term.bold('─── Resultado ─────────────────────────────────────────────\n');
388.             printColoredJson(current);
389.             term('\n');
390.             term.bold('────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────\n');
391. 
392.             if (isDryRun) {
393.                 term.yellow('  (modo dry-run — não será salvo no banco)\n');
394.             }
395. 
396.             term('\n');
397.             term.cyan('Glossário ');
398.             term.gray('(formato: "termo > tradução ; outro > outro" — vazio para confirmar)');
399.             term.cyan(': ');
400. 
401.             const input = await new Promise<string>((resolve) => {
402.                 term.inputField({}, (_, value) => {
403.                     term('\n');
404.                     resolve((value ?? '').trim());
405.                 });
406.             });
407. 
408.             // Empty input = confirm
409.             if (!input) {
410.                 return current;
411.             }
412. 
413.             // Parse and validate
414.             const { entries: newEntries, errors } = parseGlossaryInput(input);
415. 
416.             if (errors.length > 0) {
417.                 for (const err of errors) {
418.                     term.red(`  ✗ ${err}\n`);
419.                 }
420.                 term.yellow('  Por favor, corrija o formato e tente novamente.\n');
421.                 continue;
422.             }
423. 
424.             if (newEntries.length === 0) {
425.                 term.yellow('  Nenhuma entrada reconhecida. Tente novamente.\n');
426.                 continue;
427.             }
428. 
429.             // Save new entries to MongoDB
430.             await saveEntries(newEntries);
431.             term.green(`  ✓ ${newEntries.length} entrada(s) salva(s) no glossário.\n`);
432. 
433.             // Reload and reapply all entries (including newly saved ones)
434.             entries = await loadAllEntries();
435.             current = this.applyGlossaryToOutput(output, entries);
436.         }
437.     }
438. 
439.     // ─── Main loop ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
440. 
441.     async run(): Promise<void> {
442.         this.log(`\nStarting provider: ${this.name}`, 'info');
443. 
444.         const items = this.readDataFile();
445.         const startIndex = this.testMode ? 0 : (await this.readProgress()) + 1;
446. 
447.         this.log(`Total items: ${items.length}`, 'dim');
448. 
449.         if (!this.testMode && startIndex >= items.length) {
450.             this.log(`All ${items.length} items already processed. Use --reset-progress to restart.`, 'warn');
451.             return;
452.         }
453. 
454.         if (this.testMode) {
455.             this.log(`\n🧪 TEST MODE: Processing only the first item (index 0)`, 'info');
456.             await this.runInteractiveItem(items[0], 0, true);
457.             return;
458.         }
459. 
460.         if (this.autoMode) {
461.             await this.runAutoLoop(items, startIndex);
462.         } else {
463.             await this.runInteractiveLoop(items, startIndex);
464.         }
465.     }
466. 
467.     // ─── Auto mode (batch, no confirmation) ──────────────────────────────────
468. 
469.     private async runAutoLoop(items: TInput[], startIndex: number): Promise<void> {
470.         this.log(
471.             startIndex > 0
472.                 ? `Resuming from index ${startIndex} (${items.length - startIndex} remaining)`
473.                 : `Starting from the beginning`,
474.             'dim'
475.         );
476. 
477.         this.initProgressBar(items.length, startIndex);
478. 
479.         // Load glossary once for the full run
480.         const entries = await loadAllEntries();
481.         if (entries.length > 0) {
482.             this.log(`Glossário carregado: ${entries.length} entrada(s)`, 'dim');
483.         }
484. 
485.         let created = 0;
486.         let skipped = 0;
487. 
488.         for (let i = startIndex; i < items.length; i++) {
489.             const item = items[i];
490. 
491.             try {
492.                 const raw = await this.processItem(item);
493. 
494.                 if (raw === null) {
495.                     this.log(`[${i}] Skipped (processItem returned null)`, 'dim');
496.                     skipped++;
497.                     await this.saveProgress(i);
498.                     this.updateProgressBar(i + 1, '(skipped)');
499.                     continue;
500.                 }
```

1. import mongoose, { Schema, Document } from "mongoose"

```
1. import type {
2.     Race,
3.     CreateRaceInput,
4.     UpdateRaceInput,
5.     RacesFilters,
6.     RacesListResponse,
7. } from "../types/races.types"
8. 
9. const API_URL = "/api/races"
10. 
11. export async function fetchRaces(
12.     params: RacesFilters = {}
13. ): Promise<RacesListResponse> {
14.     const query = new URLSearchParams()
15. 
16.     if (params.page) query.append("page", params.page.toString())
17.     if (params.limit) query.append("limit", params.limit.toString())
18.     if (params.search) query.append("search", params.search)
19.     if (params.status && params.status !== "all") query.append("status", params.status)
20. 
21.     const res = await fetch(`${API_URL}?${query.toString()}`)
22. 
23.     if (!res.ok) {
24.         const error = await res.json().catch(() => ({ error: "Erro desconhecido" }))
25.         throw new Error(error.error || "Erro ao buscar raças")
26.     }
27. 
28.     return res.json()
29. }
30. 
31. export async function fetchRace(id: string): Promise<Race> {
32.     const res = await fetch(`${API_URL}/${id}`)
33. 
34.     if (!res.ok) {
35.         if (res.status === 404) throw new Error("Raça não encontrada")
36.         throw new Error("Erro ao buscar raça")
37.     }
38. 
39.     return res.json()
40. }
41. 
42. export async function createRace(data: CreateRaceInput): Promise<Race> {
43.     const res = await fetch(API_URL, {
44.         method: "POST",
45.         headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json" },
46.         body: JSON.stringify(data),
47.     })
48. 
49.     if (!res.ok) {
50.         const error = await res.json().catch(() => ({ error: "Erro desconhecido" }))
51.         throw new Error(error.error || "Erro ao criar raça")
52.     }
53. 
54.     return res.json()
55. }
56. 
57. export async function updateRace(id: string, data: UpdateRaceInput): Promise<Race> {
58.     const res = await fetch(`${API_URL}/${id}`, {
59.         method: "PUT",
60.         headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json" },
61.         body: JSON.stringify(data),
62.     })
63. 
64.     if (!res.ok) {
65.         const error = await res.json().catch(() => ({ error: "Erro desconhecido" }))
66.         throw new Error(error.error || "Erro ao atualizar raça")
67.     }
68. 
69.     return res.json()
70. }
71. 
72. export async function deleteRace(id: string): Promise<void> {
73.     const res = await fetch(`${API_URL}/${id}`, { method: "DELETE" })
74. 
75.     if (!res.ok) {
76.         const error = await res.json().catch(() => ({ error: "Erro desconhecido" }))
77.         throw new Error(error.error || "Erro ao excluir raça")
78.     }
79. }
80.
```

500.                 }
501. 
502.                 // Always apply glossary post-processing
503.                 const output = this.applyGlossaryToOutput(raw, entries);
504. 
505.                 const exists = await this.findExisting(output);
506.                 if (exists !== null) {
507.                     const diffs = this.diffObjects(exists, output);
508.                     if (diffs.length > 0) {
509.                         this.log(`[${i}] Conflito: ${diffs.length} campo(s) diferente(s) — mantendo existente (use modo interativo para resolver)`, 'warn');
510.                     } else {
511.                         this.log(`[${i}] Already exists — skipping`, 'dim');
512.                     }
513.                     skipped++;
514.                 } else {
515.                     await this.create(output);
516.                     this.log(`[${i}] Created successfully`, 'success');
517.                     created++;
518.                 }
519. 
520.                 await this.saveProgress(i);
521.                 this.updateProgressBar(i + 1, this.getItemLabel(output));
522.             } catch (err) {
523.                 this.stopProgressBar();
524.                 const message = err instanceof Error ? err.message : String(err);
525.                 this.log(`\nFatal error at index ${i}: ${message}`, 'error');
526.                 this.log(`Script stopped. Fix the issue and re-run — it will resume from index ${i}.`, 'warn');
527.                 throw err;
528.             }
529.         }
530. 
531.         this.stopProgressBar();
532. 
533.         term('\n\n');
534.         term.bold(`─── ${this.name} Summary ───────────────────────────\n`);
535.         term.green(`  Created:  ${created}\n`);
536.         term.yellow(`  Skipped:  ${skipped}\n`);
537.         term(`  Total processed: ${items.length - startIndex}\n`);
538.         term.bold(`────────────────────────────────────────────────\n`);
539.     }
540. 
541.     // ─── Interactive mode (one item at a time with review) ────────────────────
542. 
543.     private async runInteractiveLoop(items: TInput[], startIndex: number): Promise<void> {
544.         this.log(
545.             startIndex > 0
546.                 ? `Resuming from index ${startIndex} (${items.length - startIndex} remaining)`
547.                 : `Starting from the beginning`,
548.             'dim'
549.         );
550. 
551.         let created = 0;
552.         let updated = 0;
553.         let skipped = 0;
554. 
555.         for (let i = startIndex; i < items.length; i++) {
556.             term('\n');
557.             term.bold(`─── Item ${i + 1} / ${items.length} ──────────────────────────────────\n`);
558. 
559.             try {
560.                 const result = await this.runInteractiveItem(items[i], i, false);
561.                 if (result === 'created') created++;
562.                 else if (result === 'updated') updated++;
563.                 else skipped++;
564.             } catch (err) {
565.                 const message = err instanceof Error ? err.message : String(err);
566.                 this.log(`\nFatal error at index ${i}: ${message}`, 'error');
567.                 this.log(`Script stopped. Fix the issue and re-run — it will resume from index ${i}.`, 'warn');
568.                 throw err;
569.             }
570.         }
571. 
572.         term('\n\n');
573.         term.bold(`─── ${this.name} Summary ───────────────────────────\n`);
574.         term.green(`  Created:  ${created}\n`);
575.         term.cyan(`  Updated:  ${updated}\n`);
576.         term.yellow(`  Skipped:  ${skipped}\n`);
577.         term(`  Total processed: ${items.length - startIndex}\n`);
578.         term.bold(`────────────────────────────────────────────────\n`);
579.     }
580. 
581.     /**
582.      * Process a single item interactively. Returns 'created', 'updated',
583.      * 'skipped', or 'exists'. In dry-run/test mode, does not save to DB.
584.      */
585.     private async runInteractiveItem(
586.         item: TInput,
587.         index: number,
588.         isDryRun: boolean,
589.     ): Promise<'created' | 'updated' | 'skipped' | 'exists'> {
590.         const raw = await this.processItem(item);
591. 
592.         if (raw === null) {
593.             term.yellow('  ⚠  Item ignorado (processItem retornou null)\n');
594.             if (!isDryRun) await this.saveProgress(index);
595.             return 'skipped';
596.         }
597. 
598.         // Apply glossary silently so findExisting uses the canonicalized name
599.         // (a previous run may have stored the item with the glossary applied,
600.         // so searching with the raw AI-translated name could miss it)
601.         const glossaryEntries = await loadAllEntries();
602.         const glossarized = this.applyGlossaryToOutput(raw, glossaryEntries);
603. 
604.         // Resolve conflicts field by field BEFORE the glossary review step
605.         const existing = await this.findExisting(glossarized);
606.         let working: TOutput = glossarized;
607. 
608.         if (existing) {
609.             const diffs = this.diffObjects(existing, glossarized);
610.             if (diffs.length > 0) {
611.                 working = await this.resolveConflictsFieldByField(existing, glossarized, diffs);
612.             } else if (!isDryRun) {
613.                 term.yellow('  ⚠  Já existe no banco e está igual — ignorando.\n');
614.                 await this.saveProgress(index);
615.                 return 'exists';
616.             }
617.         }
618. 
619.         // Interactive review: show result, allow glossary corrections
620.         const final = await this.reviewAndConfirmItem(working, isDryRun);
621. 
622.         if (isDryRun) {
623.             term.green('\n✓ Modo dry-run — nenhum dado foi salvo.\n');
624.             return 'skipped';
625.         }
626. 
627.         if (existing) {
628.             const finalDiffs = this.diffObjects(existing, final);
629.             if (finalDiffs.length === 0) {
630.                 term.yellow('  ⚠  Resultado igual ao existente — ignorando.\n');
631.                 await this.saveProgress(index);
632.                 return 'exists';
633.             }
634.             await this.update(final);
635.             term.green('  ✓ Atualizado com sucesso.\n');
636.             await this.saveProgress(index);
637.             return 'updated';
638.         }
639. 
640.         await this.create(final);
641.         term.green(`  ✓ Criado com sucesso.\n`);
642.         await this.saveProgress(index);
643.         return 'created';
644.     }
645. 
646.     // ─── Abstract methods ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────
647. 
648.     /**
649.      * Map and translate a single 5etools item into the system input format.
650.      * Return null to skip the item entirely.
651.      */
652.     abstract processItem(item: TInput): Promise<TOutput | null>;
653. 
654.     /**
655.      * Find an existing item in the database that matches the incoming item.
656.      * Returns the existing item's data (as TOutput) or null if not found.
657.      */
658.     abstract findExisting(item: TOutput): Promise<TOutput | null>;
659. 
660.     /**
661.      * Insert the item into the database.
662.      */
663.     abstract create(item: TOutput): Promise<void>;
664. 
665.     /**
666.      * Update an existing item in the database.
667.      * Override in subclasses that support conflict resolution updates.
668.      */
669.     async update(_item: TOutput): Promise<void> {
670.         this.log('update() not implemented for this provider — skipping.', 'warn');
671.     }
672. 
673.     /**
674.      * Return a human-readable label for the progress bar (e.g. spell name).
675.      * Override in subclasses for better output.
676.      */
677.     getItemLabel(item: TOutput): string {
678.         const obj = item as Record<string, unknown>;
679.         return String(obj['name'] ?? '');
680.     }
681. }
682.

```
1. "use client";
2. 
3. import { useQuery, useMutation, useQueryClient, useInfiniteQuery } from "@tanstack/react-query"
4. import type { 
5.     Race, 
6.     CreateRaceInput, 
7.     UpdateRaceInput, 
8.     RacesFilters, 
9.     RacesListResponse 
10. } from "../types/races.types"
11. import { 
12.     fetchRaces, 
13.     fetchRace, 
14.     createRace, 
15.     updateRace, 
16.     deleteRace 
17. } from "./races-api"
18. 
19. export const racesKeys = {
20.     all: ["races"] as const,
21.     lists: () => [...racesKeys.all, "list"] as const,
22.     list: (filters: RacesFilters) => [...racesKeys.lists(), filters] as const,
23.     infinite: (filters: RacesFilters) => [...racesKeys.all, "infinite", filters] as const,
24.     details: () => [...racesKeys.all, "detail"] as const,
25.     detail: (id: string) => [...racesKeys.details(), id] as const,
26. }
27. 
28. export function useRaces(
29.     filters: RacesFilters = {},
30.     page = 1,
31.     limit = 10,
32.     options: { enabled?: boolean } = {}
33. ) {
34.     return useQuery<RacesListResponse, Error>({
35.         queryKey: racesKeys.list({ ...filters, page, limit }),
36.         queryFn: () => fetchRaces({ ...filters, page, limit }),
37.         staleTime: 30 * 1000,
38.         ...options,
39.     })
40. }
41. 
42. export function useInfiniteRaces(
43.     filters: RacesFilters = {},
44.     options: { enabled?: boolean; limit?: number } = {}
45. ) {
46.     const limit = options.limit || 10
47. 
48.     return useInfiniteQuery({
49.         queryKey: racesKeys.infinite({ ...filters, limit }),
50.         queryFn: async ({ pageParam = 1 }) => fetchRaces({ ...filters, page: pageParam as number, limit }),
51.         initialPageParam: 1,
52.         getNextPageParam: (lastPage) => {
53.             const totalPages = Math.ceil(lastPage.total / lastPage.limit)
54.             return lastPage.page < totalPages ? lastPage.page + 1 : undefined
55.         },
56.         ...options,
57.     })
58. }
59. 
60. export function useRace(id: string | null) {
61.     return useQuery<Race, Error>({
62.         queryKey: racesKeys.detail(id || ""),
63.         queryFn: () => fetchRace(id!),
64.         enabled: !!id,
65.         staleTime: 60 * 1000,
66.     })
67. }
68. 
69. export function useCreateRace() {
70.     const queryClient = useQueryClient()
71. 
72.     return useMutation({
73.         mutationFn: (data: CreateRaceInput) => createRace(data),
74.         onSuccess: () => {
75.             queryClient.invalidateQueries({ queryKey: racesKeys.all })
76.             queryClient.invalidateQueries({ queryKey: ["audit-logs"] })
77.             queryClient.invalidateQueries({ queryKey: ["dashboard-stats"] })
78.         },
79.     })
80. }
81. 
82. export function useUpdateRace() {
83.     const queryClient = useQueryClient()
84. 
85.     return useMutation({
86.         mutationFn: ({ id, data }: { id: string; data: UpdateRaceInput }) => updateRace(id, data),
87.         onSuccess: () => {
88.             queryClient.invalidateQueries({ queryKey: racesKeys.all })
89.             queryClient.invalidateQueries({ queryKey: ["audit-logs"] })
90.             queryClient.invalidateQueries({ queryKey: ["dashboard-stats"] })
91.         },
92.     })
93. }
94. 
95. export function useDeleteRace() {
96.     const queryClient = useQueryClient()
97. 
98.     return useMutation({
99.         mutationFn: (id: string) => deleteRace(id),
100.         onSuccess: () => {
101.             queryClient.invalidateQueries({ queryKey: racesKeys.all })
102.             queryClient.invalidateQueries({ queryKey: ["audit-logs"] })
103.             queryClient.invalidateQueries({ queryKey: ["dashboard-stats"] })
104.         },
105.     })
106. }
107.
```

```
1. /**
2.  * @fileoverview Seed Data Script — Entry Point
3.  *
4.  * Loads environment, connects to MongoDB, lets the user select a provider
5.  * and a translation provider via terminal-kit menus, and runs it.
6.  *
7.  * Usage:
8.  *   tsx scripts/seed-data/index.ts [flags]
9.  *
10.  * Run with --help to see all available flags.
11.  * To reset progress for a provider, run with --reset-progress.
12.  */
13. 
14. import dotenv from 'dotenv';
15. import path from 'path';
16. import mongoose from 'mongoose';
17. import terminal from 'terminal-kit';
18. 
19. // Type-only imports — erased at compile time, generate no require() calls.
20. import type { BaseProvider } from './base-provider';
21. import type { BaseTranslator, RateLimitConfig, LibreTranslateTranslator as LibreTranslateTranslatorType } from './translation';
22. import { countEntries, clearAllEntries, backupGlossary, restoreGlossary } from './glossary/glossary-store';
23. import { listAllProgress, resetProgress } from './progress/progress-store';
24. 
25. // Load .env FIRST — must happen before requiring any module that reads env vars
26. // at load time (e.g. src/core/ai/genai.ts reads GOOGLE_API_KEY at module level).
27. dotenv.config({ path: path.resolve(__dirname, '../../.env') });
28. 
29. // eslint-disable-next-line @typescript-eslint/no-require-imports
30. const { SpellsProvider } = require('./providers/spells-provider') as typeof import('./providers/spells-provider');
31. // eslint-disable-next-line @typescript-eslint/no-require-imports
32. const { ALL_TRANSLATORS, GenAITranslator, LibreTranslateTranslator } = require('./translation') as typeof import('./translation');
33. 
34. const term = terminal.terminal;
35. 
36. // ─── Register providers here ──────────────────────────────────────────────────
37. // When new providers are created, just add them to this array.
38. 
39. const providers: BaseProvider<unknown, unknown>[] = [
40.     new SpellsProvider(),
41. ];
42. 
43. // ─── Database ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
44. 
45. async function connectDatabase(): Promise<void> {
46.     const mongoUri = process.env.MONGODB_URI;
47.     if (!mongoUri) {
48.         throw new Error('MONGODB_URI environment variable is not set. Check your .env file.');
49.     }
50.     await mongoose.connect(mongoUri);
51. }
52. 
53. // ─── Help ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
54. 
55. function printHelp(): void {
56.     term.bold.cyan('\n🎲 D&D Seed Data Script\n');
57.     term('─────────────────────────────────────────\n\n');
58. 
59.     term.bold('Uso:\n');
60.     term('  tsx scripts/seed-data/index.ts [flags]\n\n');
61. 
62.     term.bold('Flags:\n');
63.     term.green('  --help             ');
64.     term('Exibe esta ajuda e encerra\n');
65.     term.green('  --list-models      ');
66.     term('Lista modelos GenAI disponíveis e encerra\n');
67.     term.green('  --clear-glossary   ');
68.     term('Backup + limpa o glossário no MongoDB e encerra\n');
69.     term.green('  --dump-glossary    ');
70.     term('Exporta o glossário via mongodump e encerra\n');
71.     term.green('  --restore-glossary ');
72.     term('[./path]  Restaura o glossário de um backup (path opcional; tab completion ✅)\n');
73.     term.green('  --reset-progress   ');
74.     term('Reseta o progresso de um provider no MongoDB e encerra\n');
75.     term.green('  --test / --dry-run ');
76.     term('Revisão interativa do 1º item, não salva no banco\n');
77.     term.green('  --auto             ');
78.     term('Processa todos os itens sem confirmação (batch)\n\n');
79. 
80.     term.bold('Modos de execução:\n\n');

### ✅ `view`

**view the file at /home/burgos/code/dndicas/src/app/api/races/route.ts.**

/home/burgos/code/dndicas/src/app/api/races/route.ts

<details>
<summary>122 lines</summary>

```
1. import { NextRequest, NextResponse } from "next/server"
2. import { auth } from "@clerk/nextjs/server"
3. import { RaceModel } from "@/features/races/models/race"
4. import dbConnect from "@/core/database/db"
5. import { z } from "zod"
6. import { createAuditLog } from "@/features/users/api/audit-service"
7. 
8. const raceTraitSchema = z.object({
9.     name: z.string().min(1),
10.     level: z.coerce.number().default(1),
11.     description: z.string().min(1),
12. })
13. 
14. const raceVariationSchema = z.object({
15.     name: z.string().min(2),
16.     description: z.string().optional().default(""),
17.     source: z.string().optional(),
18.     image: z.string().optional(),
19.     color: z.string().optional(),
20.     traits: z.array(raceTraitSchema).default([]),
21.     spells: z.array(z.any()).default([]),
22.     size: z.enum(["Pequeno", "Médio", "Grande"]).optional(),
23.     speed: z.string().optional(),
24. })
25. 
26. const raceSchema = z.object({
27.     name: z.string().min(2).max(100),
28.     description: z.string().min(10),
29.     source: z.string(),
30.     status: z.enum(["active", "inactive"]),
31.     image: z.string().optional(),
32.     size: z.enum(["Pequeno", "Médio", "Grande"]),
33.     speed: z.string().min(1),
34.     traits: z.array(raceTraitSchema).default([]),
35.     spells: z.array(z.any()).default([]),
36.     variations: z.array(raceVariationSchema).default([]),
37. })
38. 
39. export async function GET(req: NextRequest) {
40.     try {
41.         await dbConnect()
42.         const url = new URL(req.url)
43.         const page = parseInt(url.searchParams.get("page") || "1", 10)
44.         const limit = parseInt(url.searchParams.get("limit") || "10", 10)
45.         const search = url.searchParams.get("search") || ""
46.         const status = url.searchParams.get("status")
47. 
48.         const query: any = {}
49.         if (search) {
50.             query.$or = [{ name: { $regex: search, $options: "i" } }, { description: { $regex: search, $options: "i" } }]
51.         }
52.         if (status && status !== "all") {
53.             query.status = status
54.         }
55. 
56.         const items = await RaceModel.find(query)
57.             .sort({ name: 1 })
58.             .skip((page - 1) * limit)
59.             .limit(limit)
60.             .lean()
61. 
62.         const formattedItems = items.map((item: any) => ({
63.             ...item,
64.             id: item._id.toString(),
65.         }))
66. 
67.         const total = await RaceModel.countDocuments(query)
68. 
69.         return NextResponse.json({
70.             items: formattedItems,
71.             total,
72.             page,
73.             limit,
74.         })
75.     } catch (error) {
76.         console.error("Races GET error:", error)
77.         return NextResponse.json({ error: "Failed to fetch races" }, { status: 500 })
78.     }
79. }
80. 
81. export async function POST(req: NextRequest) {
82.     try {
83.         const { userId } = await auth()
84.         // if (!userId) return NextResponse.json({ error: "Unauthorized" }, { status: 401 })
85. 
86.         const body = await req.json()
87. 
88.         // Normalize traits for Mongoose
89.         if (body.traits && Array.isArray(body.traits)) {
90.             body.traits = body.traits.map((t: any) => ({
91.                 name: t.name && t.name.trim() !== "" ? t.name : "Traço Racial",
92.                 level: t.level || 1,
93.                 description: t.description,
94.             }))
95.         }
96. 
97.         const validated = raceSchema.parse(body)
98.         await dbConnect()
99. 
100.         const race = await RaceModel.create(validated)
101. 
102.         // Audit configuration
103.         if (userId) {
104.             await createAuditLog({
105.                 performedBy: userId,
106.                 action: "CREATE",
107.                 entity: "Race",
108.                 entityId: race._id.toString(),
109.                 newData: (race.toObject ? race.toObject() : race) as any,
110.             })
111.         }
112. 
113.         return NextResponse.json(race)
114.     } catch (error) {
115.         if (error instanceof z.ZodError) {
116.             return NextResponse.json({ error: error.flatten().fieldErrors }, { status: 400 })
117.         }
118.         console.error("Races POST error:", error)
119.         return NextResponse.json({ error: "Failed to create race" }, { status: 500 })
120.     }
121. }
122.
```

</details>

<sub>⏱️ 20m 24s</sub>

### ✅ `bash`

**Analyze races data distribution**

$ cd /home/burgos/code/dndicas && cat src/lib/5etools-data/races.json | python3 -c "
import json,sys
d=json.load(sys.stdin)

# Check race sources distribution
races = d.get('race', [])
sources = {}
for r in races:
    s = r.get('source', 'unknown')
    sources[s] = sources.get(s, 0) + 1
print('Race sources:', sources)

# Check races with hasFluffImages
with_images = [r for r in races if r.get('hasFluffImages')]
print(f'Races with images: {len(with_images)} of {len(races)}')

# Check speed types
for r in races[:5]:
    print(f'{r[\"name\"]}: speed={r.get(\"speed\")}, size={r.get(\"size\")}')
"

/home/burgos/code/dndicas/src/features/spells/api/spells-service.ts

<summary>328 lines</summary>

````
1. /**
2.  * @fileoverview Service layer for Spells management with CRUD operations and audit logging.
3.  *
4.  * @see specs/004-spells-catalog/spec.md - FR-004 to FR-010
5.  */
6. 
7. import dbConnect from '@/core/database/db';
8. import { Spell, type ISpell } from '../models/spell';
9. import { logCreate, logUpdate, logDelete } from '@/features/users/api/audit-service';
10. import { applyFuzzySearch } from "@/core/utils/search-engine"
11. import type {
12.   CreateSpellInput,
13.   UpdateSpellInput,
14.   SpellsFilters,
15.   SpellsListResponse,
16. } from '../types/spells.types';
17. 
18. /**
19.  * List spells with filters and pagination.
20.  *
21.  * @param filters - Query filters (search, circles, schools, saveAttributes, diceTypes, status)
22.  * @param page - Current page number (1-based)
23.  * @param limit - Items per page
24.  * @param isAdmin - Whether the requester is an admin (admins see all statuses)
25.  * @returns Paginated list of spells
26.  *
27.  * @example
28.  * ```ts
29.  * const result = await listSpells(
30.  *   { search: 'fogo', circles: [3], schools: ['Evocação'] },
31.  *   1,
32.  *   10,
33.  *   false
34.  * );
35.  * ```
36.  */
37. export async function listSpells(filters: SpellsFilters, page = 1, limit = 10, isAdmin = false): Promise<SpellsListResponse> {
38.     try {
39.         await dbConnect()
40. 
41.         // Build query
42.         const query: Record<string, unknown> = {}
43. 
44.         // Circle filter
45.         if (filters.circles && filters.circles.length > 0) {
46.             query.circle = { $in: filters.circles }
47.         }
48. 
49.         // School filter
50.         if (filters.schools && filters.schools.length > 0) {
51.             query.school = { $in: filters.schools }
52.         }
53. 
54.         // Save attribute filter
55.         if (filters.saveAttributes && filters.saveAttributes.length > 0) {
56.             query.saveAttribute = { $in: filters.saveAttributes }
57.         }
58. 
59.         // Dice type filter (base dice or extra dice per level)
60.         if (filters.diceTypes && filters.diceTypes.length > 0) {
61.             query.$or = [{ "baseDice.tipo": { $in: filters.diceTypes } }, { "extraDicePerLevel.tipo": { $in: filters.diceTypes } }]
62.         }
63. 
64.         // Status filter
65.         if (!isAdmin) {
66.             query.status = "active"
67.         } else if (filters.status) {
68.             query.status = filters.status
69.         }
70. 
71.         // Fetch ALL items matching filters (except search) to apply fuzzy search locally
72.         const items = await Spell.find(query).sort({ circle: 1, name: 1 }).lean()
73. 
74.         // Apply fuzzy search locally using the shared function
75.         const searchedItems = filters.search ? applyFuzzySearch(items, filters.search) : items
76. 
77.         const total = searchedItems.length
78.         const totalPages = limit ? Math.ceil(total / limit) : 1
79. 
80.         // Manual pagination
81.         const offset = (page - 1) * limit
82.         const paginatedItems = searchedItems.slice(offset, offset + limit)
83. 
84.         return {
85.             spells: paginatedItems.map((spell: any) => {
86.                 // Ensure component migration from "Verboso" to "Verbal"
87.                 if (spell.component && Array.isArray(spell.component)) {
88.                     spell.component = spell.component.map((comp: string) => (comp === "Verboso" ? "Verbal" : comp))
89.                 }
90. 
91.                 return {
92.                     ...spell,
93.                     _id: String(spell._id),
94.                     circleLabel: spell.circle === 0 ? "Truque" : `${spell.circle}º Círculo`,
95.                 }
96.             }),
97.             total,
98.             page,
99.             limit,
100.             totalPages,
101.         }
102.     } catch (error) {
103.         console.error("[SpellsService] Error listing spells:", error)
104.         throw new Error("Erro ao listar magias. Por favor, tente novamente.")
105.     }
106. }
107. 
108. /**
109.  * Get a single spell by ID.
110.  *
111.  * @param id - Spell ID
112.  * @param isAdmin - Whether the requester is an admin
113.  * @returns Spell document or null if not found
114.  * @throws Error if spell is inactive and requester is not admin
115.  *
116.  * @example
117.  * ```ts
118.  * const spell = await getSpellById('507f1f77bcf86cd799439011', false);
119.  * ```
120.  */
121. export async function getSpellById(id: string, isAdmin = false): Promise<ISpell | null> {
122.     try {
123.         await dbConnect()
124. 
125.         const spell = await Spell.findById(id).lean()
126. 
127.         if (!spell) {
128.             return null
129.         }
130. 
131.         // Non-admins can only see active spells
132.         if (!isAdmin && spell.status === "inactive") {
133.             throw new Error("Magia não encontrada ou inativa.")
134.         }
135. 
136.         // Ensure component migration from "Verboso" to "Verbal"
137.         if (spell.component && Array.isArray(spell.component)) {
138.             spell.component = (spell.component as string[]).map((comp) => (comp === "Verboso" ? "Verbal" : comp))
139.         }
140. 
141.         return {
142.             ...spell,
143.             _id: String(spell._id),
144.             circleLabel: spell.circle === 0 ? "Truque" : `${spell.circle}º Círculo`,
145.         } as any
146.     } catch (error) {
147.         if (error instanceof Error && error.message.includes("não encontrada")) {
148.             throw error
149.         }
150.         console.error("[SpellsService] Error fetching spell:", error)
151.         throw new Error("Erro ao buscar magia. Por favor, tente novamente.")
152.     }
153. }
154. 
155. /**
156.  * Create a new spell with audit logging.
157.  *
158.  * @param input - Spell creation data
159.  * @param userId - ID of the user creating the spell
160.  * @returns Created spell document
161.  * @throws Error if validation fails or creation fails
162.  *
163.  * @example
164.  * ```ts
165.  * const spell = await createSpell({
166.  *   name: 'Bola de Fogo',
167.  *   description: 'Uma explosão de fogo...',
168.  *   circle: 3,
169.  *   school: 'Evocação',
170.  *   baseDice: { quantidade: 8, tipo: 'd6' },
171.  *   status: 'active'
172.  * }, 'clerkUserId123');
173.  * ```
174.  */
175. export async function createSpell(
176.   input: CreateSpellInput,
177.   userId: string
178. ): Promise<ISpell> {
179.   try {
180.     await dbConnect();
181. 
182.     // Create spell
183.     const spell = await Spell.create(input);
184. 
185.     // Audit log
186.     await logCreate(
187.       'Spell',
188.       String(spell._id),
189.       userId,
190.       spell.toObject()
191.     );
192. 
193.     return {
194.       ...spell.toObject(),
195.       _id: String(spell._id),
196.       circleLabel: spell.circle === 0 ? 'Truque' : `${spell.circle}º Círculo`,
197.     };
198.   } catch (error) {
199.     console.error('[SpellsService] Error creating spell:', error);
200. 
201.     // Handle duplicate name error
202.     if (error instanceof Error && 'code' in error && error.code === 11000) {
203.       throw new Error('Já existe uma magia com este nome.');
204.     }
205. 
206.     throw new Error('Erro ao criar magia. Por favor, tente novamente.');
207.   }
208. }
209. 
210. /**
211.  * Update an existing spell with audit logging.
212.  *
213.  * @param id - Spell ID
214.  * @param input - Spell update data (partial)
215.  * @param userId - ID of the user updating the spell
216.  * @returns Updated spell document or null if not found
217.  * @throws Error if update fails
218.  *
219.  * @example
220.  * ```ts
221.  * const spell = await updateSpell(
222.  *   '507f1f77bcf86cd799439011',
223.  *   { description: 'Descrição atualizada', status: 'inactive' },
224.  *   'clerkUserId123'
225.  * );
226.  * ```
227.  */
228. export async function updateSpell(
229.   id: string,
230.   input: UpdateSpellInput,
231.   userId: string
232. ): Promise<ISpell | null> {
233.   try {
234.     await dbConnect();
235. 
236.     // Fetch previous state for audit log
237.     const previousSpell = await Spell.findById(id).lean();
238. 
239.     if (!previousSpell) {
240.       return null;
241.     }
242. 
243.     // Update spell
244.     const updatedSpell = await Spell.findByIdAndUpdate(
245.       id,
246.       { $set: input },
247.       { new: true, runValidators: true }
248.     ).lean();
249. 
250.     if (!updatedSpell) {
251.       return null;
252.     }
253. 
254.     // Audit log
255.     await logUpdate(
256.       'Spell',
257.       String(updatedSpell._id),
258.       userId,
259.       previousSpell,
260.       updatedSpell
261.     );
262. 
263.     return {
264.       ...updatedSpell,
265.       _id: String(updatedSpell._id),
266.       circleLabel: updatedSpell.circle === 0 ? 'Truque' : `${updatedSpell.circle}º Círculo`,
267.     };
268.   } catch (error) {
269.     console.error('[SpellsService] Error updating spell:', error);
270. 
271.     // Handle duplicate name error
272.     if (error instanceof Error && 'code' in error && error.code === 11000) {
273.       throw new Error('Já existe uma magia com este nome.');
274.     }
275. 
276.     throw new Error('Erro ao atualizar magia. Por favor, tente novamente.');
277.   }
278. }
279. 
280. /**
281.  * Delete a spell with audit logging.
282.  *
283.  * @param id - Spell ID
284.  * @param userId - ID of the user deleting the spell
285.  * @returns Deleted spell document or null if not found
286.  * @throws Error if deletion fails
287.  *
288.  * @example
289.  * ```ts
290.  * const deleted = await deleteSpell('507f1f77bcf86cd799439011', 'clerkUserId123');
291.  * ```
292.  */
293. export async function deleteSpell(
294.   id: string,
295.   userId: string
296. ): Promise<ISpell | null> {
297.   try {
298.     await dbConnect();
299. 
300.     // Fetch spell for audit log before deletion
301.     const spell = await Spell.findById(id).lean();
302. 
303.     if (!spell) {
304.       return null;
305.     }
306. 
307.     // Delete spell
308.     await Spell.findByIdAndDelete(id);
309. 
310.     // Audit log
311.     await logDelete(
312.       'Spell',
313.       String(spell._id),
314.       userId,
315.       spell
316.     );
317. 
318.     return {
319.       ...spell,
320.       _id: String(spell._id),
321.       circleLabel: spell.circle === 0 ? 'Truque' : `${spell.circle}º Círculo`,
322.     };
323.   } catch (error) {
324.     console.error('[SpellsService] Error deleting spell:', error);
325.     throw new Error('Erro ao excluir magia. Por favor, tente novamente.');
326.   }
327. }
328.

<sub>⏱️ 31m 0s</sub>

### 💬 Copilot

Done! Here's what was implemented:

### Created `scripts/seed-data/providers/races-provider.ts`
- Extends `BaseProvider\<FiveEToolsRace, CreateRaceInput\>`
- Overrides `readDataFile()` to also load the `subrace[]` array from the JSON
- **Filtering:** skips races tagged `"NPC Race"` or with `reprintedAs` (superseded) — processes ~94 of 158 races
- **Speed:** maps ft→m for numbers and objects (walk/fly/swim/climb/burrow), handles `fly: true` ("voo igual ao deslocamento a pé")
- **Size:** `M`→`Médio`, `S`→`Pequeno`, `L`→`Grande`
- **Image:** `https://5e.tools/img/{source}/{name}.webp` when `hasFluffImages === true`
- **Description:** full HTML built from entries, translated via `translateItem`
- **Variations:** matching subraces are each translated and mapped to `RaceVariation[]`
- Direct `RaceModel` access for `create` / `update` / `findExisting`

### Edited `scripts/seed-data/index.ts`
- Registered `RacesProvider` in the providers array — it will appear in the interactive selector when running `tsx scripts/seed-data/index.ts`

## RacesProvider implemented ✅

### Created `scripts/seed-data/providers/races-provider.ts`
Full provider extending `BaseProvider<FiveEToolsRace, CreateRaceInput>` with:

- **Filtering**: skips `"NPC Race"` tagged races and races with `reprintedAs` set (~94 of 158 races processed)
- **`readDataFile()` override**: loads both `race[]` and `subrace[]` arrays from `races.json` in one pass
- **Speed mapping**: ft→m conversion for number or `{walk, fly, swim, climb, burrow}` objects (including `fly: true` → "voo igual ao deslocamento a pé")
- **Size mapping**: `M`→`Médio`, `S`→`Pequeno`, `L`→`Grande`

- **Variations**: up to 97 subraces matched by `raceName + raceSource`, each translated separately and mapped to `RaceVariation[]`

### ✓ Task Complete

## RacesProvider implemented ✅

### Created `scripts/seed-data/providers/races-provider.ts`
Full provider extending `BaseProvider<FiveEToolsRace, CreateRaceInput>` with:

- **Filtering**: skips `"NPC Race"` tagged races and races with `reprintedAs` set (~94 of 158 races processed)
- **`readDataFile()` override**: loads both `race[]` and `subrace[]` arrays from `races.json` in one pass
- **Speed mapping**: ft→m conversion for number or `{walk, fly, swim, climb, burrow}` objects (including `fly: true` → "voo igual ao deslocamento a pé")
- **Size mapping**: `M`→`Médio`, `S`→`Pequeno`, `L`→`Grande`
- **Image**: `https://5e.tools/img/{source}/{name}.webp` when `hasFluffImages === true` (per base-provider comment)
- **Description**: HTML built from entries and translated via `translateItem`, with feet→meters post-processing
- **Variations**: up to 97 subraces matched by `raceName + raceSource`, each translated separately and mapped to `RaceVariation[]`
- **DB ops**: direct `RaceModel.create/findOneAndUpdate/findOne` (no HTTP service layer)

### Edited `scripts/seed-data/index.ts`
Registered `RacesProvider` in the providers array — appears in the interactive menu when running:
```
tsx scripts/seed-data/index.ts
```

TypeScript type-check passes with zero errors.

1. /**
2.  * Teste exemplo para o storage utility
3.  */
4. 
5. import { storage } from '@/core/utils/storage';
6. 
7. describe('Storage Utility', () => {
8.   beforeEach(() => {
9.     // Limpa o storage antes de cada teste
10.     localStorage.clear();
11.   });
12. 
13.   describe('set and get', () => {
14.     it('should store and retrieve a string value', () => {
15.       storage.set('testKey', 'testValue');
16.       const value = storage.get<string>('testKey');
17.       expect(value).toBe('testValue');
18.     });
19. 
20.     it('should store and retrieve an object', () => {
21.       const testObject = { name: 'Test', age: 25 };
22.       storage.set('testObject', testObject);
23.       const value = storage.get<typeof testObject>('testObject');
24.       expect(value).toEqual(testObject);
25.     });
26. 
27.     it('should return default value when key does not exist', () => {
28.       const value = storage.get('nonexistent', 'default');
29.       expect(value).toBe('default');
30.     });
31.   });
32. 
33.   describe('remove', () => {
34.     it('should remove a stored value', () => {
35.       storage.set('testKey', 'testValue');
36.       storage.remove('testKey');
37.       const value = storage.get('testKey');
38.       expect(value).toBeNull();
39.     });
40.   });
41. 
42.   describe('has', () => {
43.     it('should return true for existing key', () => {
44.       storage.set('testKey', 'value');
45.       expect(storage.has('testKey')).toBe(true);
46.     });
47. 
48.     it('should return false for non-existing key', () => {
49.       expect(storage.has('nonexistent')).toBe(false);
50.     });
51.   });
52. 
53.   describe('keys', () => {
54.     it('should return all storage keys', () => {
55.       storage.set('key1', 'value1');
56.       storage.set('key2', 'value2');
57.       const keys = storage.keys();
58.       expect(keys).toContain('key1');
59.       expect(keys).toContain('key2');
60.     });
61.   });
62. 
63.   describe('clear', () => {
64.     it('should clear all app storage', () => {
65.       storage.set('key1', 'value1');
66.       storage.set('key2', 'value2');
67.       storage.clear();
68.       expect(storage.keys()).toHaveLength(0);
69.     });
70.   });
71. });
72.

### ✅ `bash`

**Rewrite plan.md**

$ cat > /home/burgos/.copilot/session-state/52979fe9-a65f-4430-8600-6981bbae2025/plan.md << 'PLANEOF'
# Plan: RacesProvider Tests (Vitest)

## Problem
Add unit + integration tests for `RacesProvider` using Vitest. The project currently uses Jest only for frontend tests; Vitest needs to be set up for the seed-data scripts.

## Approach
1. Install Vitest + needed TS support
2. Create `vitest.config.ts` at repo root for script tests
3. Export pure helper functions from `races-provider.ts` for isolated unit testing
4. Write test file `scripts/seed-data/providers/__tests__/races-provider.test.ts`
5. Add `test:seed` script to `package.json`

---

## Files

| Action | File |
|--------|------|
| **EDIT** | `package.json` — add vitest devDep + `test:seed` script |
| **CREATE** | `vitest.config.ts` |
| **EDIT** | `scripts/seed-data/providers/races-provider.ts` — export pure helpers |
| **CREATE** | `scripts/seed-data/providers/__tests__/races-provider.test.ts` |

---

## Vitest Config
- `include`: `scripts/**/*.test.ts`
- `environment`: `node` (not jsdom — no DOM needed)
- `resolve.alias`: `@/ → ./src/` (same as tsconfig paths)

## Helpers to Export (pure functions, no side effects)
- `mapSize(sizeArr)` → `SizeCategory`
- `mapSpeed(speed)` → `string`
- `cleanText(text)` → `string`
- `buildDescriptionHtml(entries)` → `string`

## Test Coverage Plan

### 1. `mapSize`
- Empty/undefined → `"Médio"`
- `['M']` → `"Médio"`
- `['S']` → `"Pequeno"`
- `['L']` → `"Grande"`
- `['S', 'M']` → `"Pequeno"` (first mappable)
- Unknown `['X']` → `"Médio"` (fallback)

### 2. `mapSpeed`
- `undefined` → `"9 metros"`
- `30` (number, feet) → `"9 metros"`
- `25` → `"7,5 metros"`
- `{ walk: 30, fly: 50 }` → `"9 metros (a pé), 15 metros (voando)"`
- `{ walk: 30, fly: true }` → `"9 metros (a pé), voo igual ao deslocamento a pé"`
- `{ walk: 25, swim: 25 }` → `"7,5 metros (a pé), 7,5 metros (nadando)"`

### 3. `cleanText`
- Strips `{@damage 1d6}` → `"1d6"`
- Strips `{@spell fireball}` → `"fireball"`
- Strips `{@condition frightened}` → `"frightened"`
- Strips `{@dc 8}` → `"CD 8"`

### 4. `buildDescriptionHtml`
- Empty/undefined → `"<p></p>"`
- String entry → `<p>text</p>`
- Named entry with sub-entries → `<p><strong>Name.</strong></p><p>text</p>`
- List entry → `<ul><li>item</li></ul>`

### 5. `processItem` (mocking `translateItem` + `fs`)
- Race with `traitTags: ["NPC Race"]` → returns `null`
- Race with `reprintedAs: ["Race|MPMM"]` → returns `null`
- Valid PHB race → returns `CreateRaceInput` with correct fields
  - name/description come from mock `translateItem`
  - size, speed, source, status mapped correctly
  - `hasFluffImages: true` → image URL set
  - `hasFluffImages` absent → image is `""`
  - `traits: []`, `spells: []`
- Race with matching subraces → `variations` array populated

### 6. `findExisting` (mocking `RaceModel` + `dbConnect`)
- No match → returns `null`
- Match found → returns mapped `CreateRaceInput`

---

## Todos
1. Install Vitest + create config
2. Export helpers from races-provider.ts
3. Write test file
PLANEOF

```

<exited with exit code 0>
```
