```
70.     hasFluffImages?: boolean;
71.     reprintedAs?: string[];
72.     _versions?: unknown[];
73. }
74. 
75. // ─── Helpers ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
76. 
77. const SIZE_MAP: Record<string, SizeCategory> = {
78.     S: 'Pequeno',
79.     M: 'Médio',
80.     L: 'Grande',
81. };
82. 
83. function mapSize(sizeArr: string[] | undefined): SizeCategory {
84.     if (!sizeArr || sizeArr.length === 0) return 'Médio';
85.     for (const s of sizeArr) {
86.         const mapped = SIZE_MAP[s];
87.         if (mapped) return mapped;
88.     }
89.     return 'Médio';
90. }
91. 
92. function feetToMetersNum(feet: number): string {
93.     const m = feet * 0.3;
94.     return Number.isInteger(m) ? String(m) : m.toFixed(1).replace('.', ',');
95. }
96. 
97. const SPEED_LABELS: Record<string, string> = {
98.     walk: 'a pé',
99.     fly: 'voando',
100.     swim: 'nadando',
101.     climb: 'escalando',
102.     burrow: 'escavando',
103. };
104. 
105. function mapSpeed(speed: number | Record<string, number | boolean> | undefined): string {
106.     if (speed === undefined) return '9 metros';
107. 
108.     if (typeof speed === 'number') {
109.         return `${feetToMetersNum(speed)} metros`;
110.     }
111. 
112.     const parts: string[] = [];
113.     for (const [key, value] of Object.entries(speed)) {
114.         const label = SPEED_LABELS[key] ?? key;
115.         if (typeof value === 'number') {
116.             parts.push(`${feetToMetersNum(value)} metros (${label})`);
117.         } else if (value === true) {
118.             // e.g. fly: true means "equal to walking speed"
119.             if (key === 'fly') {
120.                 parts.push('voo igual ao deslocamento a pé');
121.             } else {
122.                 parts.push(`deslocamento de ${label} igual ao deslocamento a pé`);
123.             }
124.         }
125.     }
126. 
127.     return parts.join(', ') || '9 metros';
128. }
129. 
130. function buildImageUrl(source: string, name: string): string {
131.     // 5etools image convention: https://5e.tools/img/{SOURCE}/{Name}.webp
132.     const encodedName = encodeURIComponent(name);
133.     return `https://5e.tools/img/${source}/${encodedName}.webp`;
134. }
135. 
136. function buildSourceLabel(source: string, page?: number): string {
137.     return page !== undefined ? `${source} pág. ${page}` : source;
138. }
139. 
140. /** Strip 5etools inline tag syntax from text before sending to AI. */
141. function cleanText(text: string): string {
142.     return text
143.         .replace(/\{@damage\s+([^}]+)\}/g, '$1')
144.         .replace(/\{@scaledamage\s+([^|]+)\|[^|]+\|([^}]+)\}/g, '$2')
145.         .replace(/\{@dice\s+([^}]+)\}/g, '$1')
146.         .replace(/\{@hit\s+([^}]+)\}/g, '+$1')
147.         .replace(/\{@dc\s+([^}]+)\}/g, 'CD $1')
148.         .replace(/\{@[a-z]+\s+([^}|]+)(?:\|[^}]*)?\}/gi, '$1')
149.         .trim();
150. }
151. 
152. function buildEntryHtml(entry: FiveEToolsEntry | string): string {
153.     if (typeof entry === 'string') {
154.         return `<p>${cleanText(entry)}</p>`;
155.     }
156. 
157.     const parts: string[] = [];
158. 
159.     if (entry.type === 'list' && Array.isArray(entry.items)) {
160.         const listItems = entry.items
161.             .map((item) => {
162.                 if (typeof item === 'string') return `<li>${cleanText(item)}</li>`;
163.                 const e = item as FiveEToolsEntry;
164.                 if (e.name && e.entry) {
165.                     return `<li><strong>${cleanText(e.name)}.</strong> ${cleanText(e.entry)}</li>`;
166.                 }
167.                 if (e.entry) return `<li>${cleanText(e.entry)}</li>`;
168.                 if (e.entries) return `<li>${(e.entries as string[]).map(cleanText).join(' ')}</li>`;
169.                 return '';
170.             })
171.             .filter(Boolean);
172.         parts.push(`<ul>${listItems.join('')}</ul>`);
173.     } else if (entry.type === 'table' && Array.isArray(entry.rows)) {
174.         // Skip complex tables in the seed description
175.     } else if (Array.isArray(entry.entries)) {
```

### ✅ `bash`

**Inspect all Aarakocra entries**

$ cd /home/burgos/code/dndicas && cat src/lib/5etools-data/races.json | python3 -c "
import json, sys
d = json.load(sys.stdin)
races = d.get('race', [])

# Show all Aarakocra entries
aarakocras = [r for r in races if r['name'] == 'Aarakocra']
for a in aarakocras:
    print(f'Source: {a[\"source\"]} | traitTags: {a.get(\"traitTags\")} | reprintedAs: {a.get(\"reprintedAs\")} | NPC: {\"NPC Race\" in (a.get(\"traitTags\") or [])}')
"

<sub>⏱️ 54m 10s</sub>

### 💬 Copilot

**O que aconteceu:**
- O `--test` mode sempre processa o **índice 0** — que é `Aarakocra (DMG)`
- O DMG Aarakocra tem `traitTags: ["NPC Race"]` no 5etools — é a versão para NPCs do Dungeon Master's Guide, não jogável
- A versão **jogável** é o `Aarakocra (MPMM)` no índice 2 — ele passaria normalmente
- O índice 1 (EEPC) também seria pulado pois tem `reprintedAs`

O problema real é que o `--test` mode do `base-provider.ts` testa **sempre o item 0**, independente de ser processável ou não. Vou planejar um fix para isso.

---

<sub>⏱️ 54m 34s</sub>

### ✅ `bash`

**Write plan.md**

$ cat > /home/burgos/.copilot/session-state/52979fe9-a65f-4430-8600-6981bbae2025/plan.md << 'PLANEOF'
# Plan: Fix --test mode to skip null items

## Problem
`BaseProvider.run()` in test mode always processes `items[0]`. For `RacesProvider`,
the first item in `races.json` is `Aarakocra (DMG)`, which is correctly tagged as
`NPC Race` and returns `null` from `processItem()`. This makes `--test`/`--dry-run`
useless for providers whose first items are always skipped.

## Approach
Change the test-mode block in `base-provider.ts` to iterate items from index 0,
skipping any that `processItem` returns null for, until it finds one that is
actually processable. Cap at a reasonable max (e.g. 20) to avoid infinite loops.

## File
- **EDIT** `scripts/seed-data/base-provider.ts`

## Change
Replace:
```ts
if (this.testMode) {
    this.log(`\n🧪 TEST MODE: Processing only the first item (index 0)`, 'info');
    await this.runInteractiveItem(items[0], 0, true);
    return;
}
```

With:
```ts
if (this.testMode) {
    this.log(`\n🧪 TEST MODE: Finding first processable item...`, 'info');
    const limit = Math.min(items.length, 20);
    for (let i = 0; i < limit; i++) {
        const result = await this.runInteractiveItem(items[i], i, true);
        if (result !== 'skipped') break;
        this.log(`  Item ${i} skipped — trying next...`, 'dim');
    }
    return;
}
```

## Notes
- `runInteractiveItem` returns `'skipped'` when `processItem` returns null
- The loop cap of 20 prevents runaway iteration on pathological data
- Existing behavior is preserved for providers where items[0] is always processable
- The update test for `races-provider.test.ts` does not need changes
PLANEOF

```

<exited with exit code 0>
```

<sub>⏱️ 66m 25s</sub>

### 💬 Copilot

Tudo resolvido. Resumo do que aconteceu e o que foi corrigido:

**Por que o Aarakocra foi ignorado?**
Ele foi ignorado corretamente — o `Aarakocra (DMG)` tem `traitTags: ["NPC Race"]` no 5etools, indicando que é uma versão para criação de NPCs pelo DM (Dungeon Master's Guide), não uma raça jogável.

**Há outro Aarakocra?**
Sim — `Aarakocra (MPMM)` no índice 2 não tem NPC tag nem `reprintedAs`. Ele seria processado normalmente em execução completa.

**Fix aplicado em `base-provider.ts`:**
O `--test` mode agora itera a partir do índice 0 e avança automaticamente até encontrar o primeiro item **não ignorado**, em vez de travar sempre no índice 0. Na próxima execução com `--dry-run`, ele vai pular automaticamente os índices 0 e 1 (NPC + reprinted) e processar o `Aarakocra (MPMM)` como teste.

---

````
## Fix: `--test` mode agora encontra o primeiro item processável ✅

### O que aconteceu
`Aarakocra (DMG)` (índice 0) foi corretamente ignorado — tem `traitTags: ["NPC Race"]` no 5etools. A versão jogável é `Aarakocra (MPMM)` (índice 2).

O problema era o `--test` mode sempre processar o índice 0, tornando o dry-run inútil quando os primeiros itens são filtrados.

### Fix aplicado em `base-provider.ts`
```ts
// Antes
this.log(`\n🧪 TEST MODE: Processing only the first item (index 0)`, 'info');
await this.runInteractiveItem(items[0], 0, true);

// Depois
this.log(`\n🧪 TEST MODE: Finding first processable item...`, 'info');
const limit = Math.min(items.length, 20);
for (let i = 0; i < limit; i++) {
    const result = await this.runInteractiveItem(items[i], i, true);
    if (result !== 'skipped') break;
    this.log(`  Item ${i} skipped — trying next...`, 'dim');
}
```

Na próxima execução com `--dry-run`, o script vai pular índices 0 e 1 automaticamente e processar o `Aarakocra (MPMM)` como teste.

### Também corrigido
Erro de TypeScript no spy do `translateItem` nos testes — troca de `as never` por `as unknown as { translateItem: ... }` com `mockImplementation(...args: unknown[])`. **39/39 testes continuam passando.**
````

</details>


---

<sub>⏱️ 66m 42s</sub>

### ✓ Task Complete

## Fix: `--test` mode agora encontra o primeiro item processável ✅

### O que aconteceu
`Aarakocra (DMG)` (índice 0) foi corretamente ignorado — tem `traitTags: ["NPC Race"]` no 5etools. A versão jogável é `Aarakocra (MPMM)` (índice 2).

O problema era o `--test` mode sempre processar o índice 0, tornando o dry-run inútil quando os primeiros itens são filtrados.

### Fix aplicado em `base-provider.ts`
```ts
// Antes
this.log(`\n🧪 TEST MODE: Processing only the first item (index 0)`, 'info');
await this.runInteractiveItem(items[0], 0, true);

// Depois
this.log(`\n🧪 TEST MODE: Finding first processable item...`, 'info');
const limit = Math.min(items.length, 20);
for (let i = 0; i < limit; i++) {
    const result = await this.runInteractiveItem(items[i], i, true);
    if (result !== 'skipped') break;
    this.log(`  Item ${i} skipped — trying next...`, 'dim');
}
```

Na próxima execução com `--dry-run`, o script vai pular índices 0 e 1 automaticamente e processar o `Aarakocra (MPMM)` como teste.

### Também corrigido
Erro de TypeScript no spy do `translateItem` nos testes — troca de `as never` por `as unknown as { translateItem: ... }` com `mockImplementation(...args: unknown[])`. **39/39 testes continuam passando.**

### 👤 User

Plan não quero que as habilidades da raça estejam escritas na descrição. Na descrição deve ser a descrição mesmo, oriunda do @src/lib/5etools-data/fluff-races.json além disso, as habilidades devem ser cadastradas (caso não existam). É o array traits. E spells também pode pedir para o usuário confirmar o que fazer após buscar e encontrar resultados. Pergunte se deseja cadastrar um novo (exemplo: Voo (Aarakocra)) ou usar o que já está cadastrado. Veja como @search-cache/src/features/races/components/race-form-modal.tsx faz e siga o fluxo pela api -\> service -\> model lembrando que esse cadastro de habilidade deve ocorrer apenas quando o usuário aceitar a tradução. o fluxo é: traduzimos os dados -\> mostramos o resultado na tela com o que hoje está na descrição sendo mapeado para o array de traits, a descrição do fluff-races no campo de descrição e a url de imagem do fluff no campo de imagem -\> o usuário insere as memórias no glossário inputando normalmente (isso deve afetar tanto o name, quanto o descrption da raça e de suas habilidades) -\> usuário envia input vazio -\> buscamos no banco trait por trait do array para verificar se já existem resultados -\> caso não haja resultados para esse trait, é cadastrado e seu objeto é atualizado com o id real -\> caso haja resultados o usuário escolhe se deseja usar um dos resultados ou o novo no formato "Voo (Aarakocra)" (essa seleção pode ser com as setinhas mesmo, mas mostre o nome e a descrição dos traits em um json bonito e um index, na seleção pode ser apenas o index com o nome -\> cadastramos a raça no banco

import json, sys
d = json.load(sys.stdin)
fluffs = d.get('raceFluff', [])
print('Total fluff entries:', len(fluffs))

# Find Aarakocra MPMM
for f in fluffs:
    if f['name'] == 'Aarakocra':
        print('Found:', f.get('source'), '| has images:', bool(f.get('images')))
        print(json.dumps(f, indent=2)[:2000])
        break
"

### ✅ `bash`

**Check fluff-races images and source matching**

$ cd /home/burgos/code/dndicas && cat src/lib/5etools-data/fluff-races.json | python3 -c "
import json, sys
d = json.load(sys.stdin)
fluffs = d.get('raceFluff', [])

# Check images structure
for f in fluffs[:5]:
    imgs = f.get('images')
    if imgs:
        print(f'{f[\"name\"]} ({f[\"source\"]}): images =', json.dumps(imgs[:1], indent=2))
        break

# Check how names match with races
fluff_keys = set((f['name'], f['source']) for f in fluffs)
print('Sample fluff keys:', list(fluff_keys)[:5])

# Check if MPMM sources exist
mpmm_fluff = [(f['name'], f['source']) for f in fluffs if f['source'] == 'MPMM']
print('MPMM fluff:', mpmm_fluff[:5])
"

### ✅ `view`

**view the file at /home/burgos/code/dndicas/src/features/races/api/validation.ts.**

<details>
<summary>39 lines</summary>

```
1. 
2. import { z } from "zod"
3. import { SizeCategory } from "../types/races.types"
4. 
5. export const raceTraitSchema = z.object({
6.     _id: z.string().optional(),
7.     name: z.string().default("Habilidade sem Nome"),
8.     level: z.coerce.number().optional().default(1),
9.     description: z.string().min(1, "Descrição da característica é obrigatória")
10. })
11. 
12. export const raceVariationSchema = z.object({
13.     _id: z.string().optional(),
14.     name: z.string().min(2, "O nome deve ter pelo menos 2 caracteres"),
15.     description: z.string().optional().default(""),
16.     source: z.string().optional(),
17.     image: z.string().optional(),
18.     color: z.string().optional(),
19.     traits: z.array(raceTraitSchema).default([]),
20.     spells: z.array(z.any()).default([]),
21.     size: z.enum(["Pequeno", "Médio", "Grande"]).optional(),
22.     speed: z.string().optional()
23. })
24. 
25. export const createRaceSchema = z.object({
26.     name: z.string().min(2, "O nome deve ter pelo menos 2 caracteres").max(100),
27.     description: z.string().min(10, "A descrição deve ter pelo menos 10 caracteres"),
28.     source: z.string().min(1, "A fonte é obrigatória"),
29.     status: z.enum(["active", "inactive"]).default("active"),
30.     image: z.string().optional(),
31.     size: z.enum(["Pequeno", "Médio", "Grande"]),
32.     speed: z.union([z.string(), z.number()]).transform(val => String(val)).pipe(z.string().min(1, "O deslocamento é obrigatório")),
33.     traits: z.array(raceTraitSchema).default([]),
34.     spells: z.array(z.any()).default([]),
35.     variations: z.array(raceVariationSchema).default([])
36. })
37. 
38. export type CreateRaceSchema = z.infer<typeof createRaceSchema>
```

```
1. import mongoose, { Schema, Document, Model } from "mongoose";
2. 
3. export interface ITrait extends Document {
4.     name: string;
5.     description: string;
6.     source: string;
7.     status: "active" | "inactive";
8.     createdAt: Date;
9.     updatedAt: Date;
10. }
11. 
12. const TraitSchema = new Schema<ITrait>(
13.     {
14.         name: {
15.             type: String,
16.             required: true,
17.             unique: true,
18.             maxlength: 100,
19.             trim: true,
20.         },
21.         description: {
22.             type: String,
23.             required: true,
24.             // Rich Text is stored as raw HTML string with mentions and S3 images
25.         },
26.         source: {
27.             type: String,
28.             required: true,
29.             maxlength: 200,
30.             trim: true,
31.         },
32.         status: {
33.             type: String,
34.             enum: ["active", "inactive"],
35.             default: "active",
36.         },
37.     },
38.     {
39.         timestamps: true,
40.         toJSON: {
41.             virtuals: true,
42.             versionKey: false,
43.             transform: (_, ret) => {
44.                 const result = {
45.                     ...ret,
46.                     id: String(ret._id),
47.                 };
48.                 return result;
49.             },
50.         },
51.         toObject: { virtuals: true },
52.     },
53. );
54. 
55. // Indexes for common queries
56. TraitSchema.index({ name: "text", description: "text" });
57. TraitSchema.index({ status: 1 });
58. 
59. export const Trait: Model<ITrait> =
60.     mongoose.models.Trait || mongoose.model<ITrait>("Trait", TraitSchema);
61.
```

```
// src/features/traits/api/traits-api.ts
import { Trait, CreateTraitInput, TraitFilterParams, TraitsResponse, UpdateTraitInput } from "../types/traits.types"

const API_URL = "/api/traits"

export async function fetchTraits(params: TraitFilterParams = {}): Promise<TraitsResponse> {
    const query = new URLSearchParams()
    if (params.page) query.append("page", params.page.toString())
    if (params.limit) query.append("limit", params.limit.toString())
    if (params.search) query.append("search", params.search)
    if (params.status && params.status !== "all") query.append("status", params.status)

    const res = await fetch(`${API_URL}?${query.toString()}`)
    if (!res.ok) {
        const error = await res.json().catch(() => ({}))
        throw new Error(error.message || "Failed to fetch traits")
    }
    return res.json()
}

export async function fetchTraitById(id: string): Promise<Trait> {
  const res = await fetch(`${API_URL}/${id}`);
  if (!res.ok) {
    if (res.status === 404) throw new Error('Trait not found');
    throw new Error('Failed to fetch trait');
  }
  return res.json();
}

export async function createTrait(data: CreateTraitInput): Promise<Trait> {
  const res = await fetch(API_URL, {
    method: 'POST',
    headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
    body: JSON.stringify(data),
  });
  if (!res.ok) {
    const error = await res.json().catch(() => ({}));
    throw new Error(error.message || 'Failed to create trait');
  }
  return res.json();
}

export async function updateTrait(id: string, data: UpdateTraitInput): Promise<Trait> {
  const res = await fetch(`${API_URL}/${id}`, {
    method: 'PUT',
    headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
    body: JSON.stringify(data),
  });
  if (!res.ok) {
    const error = await res.json().catch(() => ({}));
    throw new Error(error.message || 'Failed to update trait');
  }
  return res.json();
}

export async function deleteTrait(id: string): Promise<void> {
  const res = await fetch(`${API_URL}/${id}`, {
    method: 'DELETE',
  });
  if (!res.ok) {
    const error = await res.json().catch(() => ({}));
    throw new Error(error.message || 'Failed to delete trait');
  }
}

export async function searchTraitsForMentions(query: string): Promise<Trait[]> {
  const res = await fetch(`${API_URL}/search?q=${encodeURIComponent(query)}`);
  if (!res.ok) {
    throw new Error('Failed to search traits');
  }
  const data = await res.json();
  return data.items || [];
}
<exited with exit code 0>
```

```
export interface Trait {
    _id: string; // Mongoose ID
    id: string; // Frontend ID (mapped from _id)
    name: string;
    description: string; // HTML content with mentions and S3 images
    source: string;
    status: 'active' | 'inactive';
    createdAt: string;
    updatedAt: string;
}

export type TraitResponse = Trait;

export interface CreateTraitInput {
    name: string;
    description: string;
    source: string;
    status: 'active' | 'inactive';
}

export interface UpdateTraitInput extends Partial<Omit<CreateTraitInput, 'name'>> {
    name?: string;
}

export interface TraitFilterParams {
    search?: string
    status?: "active" | "inactive" | "all"
    page?: number
    limit?: number
}

export interface TraitsResponse {
    items: Trait[];
    total: number;
    page: number;
    limit: number;
}
<exited with exit code 0>
```

### ✅ `bash`

**Check traits API route for create**

$ cat /home/burgos/code/dndicas/src/app/api/traits/route.ts | head -60

<details>
<summary>52 lines</summary>

```
import { NextRequest, NextResponse } from "next/server";
import { auth } from "@clerk/nextjs/server";
import { Trait } from "@/features/traits/database/trait";
import { createAuditLog } from "@/features/users/api/audit-service";
import dbConnect from "@/core/database/db";
import { applyFuzzySearch } from "@/core/utils/search-engine"
import { z } from "zod";

const createTraitSchema = z.object({
  name: z.string().min(3).max(100),
  description: z.string().min(10).max(50000), // HTML string with S3 images
  source: z.string().min(1).max(200),
  status: z.enum(["active", "inactive"]),
});

export async function GET(req: NextRequest) {
  try {
    await dbConnect();
    const url = new URL(req.url);
    const page = parseInt(url.searchParams.get("page") || "1", 10);
    const limit = parseInt(url.searchParams.get("limit") || "10", 10);
    const search = url.searchParams.get("search") || "";
    const searchField = url.searchParams.get("searchField") || "all";
    const status = url.searchParams.get("status");

    const query: Record<string, unknown> = {}
    if (status && status !== "all") {
        if (status === "active" || status === "inactive") {
            query.status = status
        }
    }

    // ALWAYS fetch items matching non-search filters (like status)
    // We fetch EVERYTHING without DB-level limit/search to let applyFuzzySearch do its job properly
    const items = await Trait.find(query as any).sort({ createdAt: -1 })

    // Apply fuzzy search locally using the shared function
    const searchedItems = search ? applyFuzzySearch(items, search) : items

    const total = searchedItems.length

    // Manual pagination if limit is provided (for table/page views)
    let paginatedItems = searchedItems
    if (limit) {
        const offset = (page - 1) * limit
        paginatedItems = searchedItems.slice(offset, offset + limit)
    }

    return NextResponse.json({
        items: paginatedItems,
        total,
        page,
        limit
    })
  } catch (error) {
    console.error("Traits GET error:", error);
    return NextResponse.json({ error: "Failed to fetch traits" }, { status: 500 });
  }
}
<exited with exit code 0>
```

```
export async function POST(req: NextRequest) {
  try {
    const session = await auth();
    if (!session || !session.userId) {
      return NextResponse.json({ error: "Unauthorized" }, { status: 401 });
    }

    const body = await req.json();
    const parseResult = createTraitSchema.safeParse(body);

    if (!parseResult.success) {
      // eslint-disable-next-line @typescript-eslint/no-explicit-any
      return NextResponse.json({ error: (parseResult.error as any).errors }, { status: 400 });
    }

    const validatedData = parseResult.data;

    await dbConnect();

    // Check uniqueness
    const existing = await Trait.findOne({ name: validatedData.name });
    if (existing) {
      return NextResponse.json({ error: "Trait name already exists" }, { status: 409 });
    }

    const newTrait = await Trait.create(validatedData);

    // Audit Log using standard service
    try {
      await createAuditLog({
        action: "CREATE",
--
    console.error("Traits POST error:", error);
    return NextResponse.json({ error: "Failed to create trait" }, { status: 500 });
  }
}
```

```
export interface RaceTrait {
    _id?: string
    name: string
    description: string // HTML string with Mentions
    level?: number
}

export type SizeCategory = "Pequeno" | "Médio" | "Grande"

export interface RaceVariation {
    _id?: string
    name: string
    description: string
    source?: string
    image?: string
    color?: string
    traits: RaceTrait[]
    spells: any[]
    size?: SizeCategory
    speed?: string
}

export interface Race {
    _id: string
    name: string
    image?: string
    description: string // HTML string from TipTap
    source: string
    status: "active" | "inactive"
    
    // Mechanics
    size: SizeCategory
    speed: string
    
    traits: RaceTrait[]
    spells: any[] // Array of spell objects (mention style)
    variations: RaceVariation[]
    
    createdAt: Date
    updatedAt: Date
}

export type CreateRaceInput = Omit<Race, "_id" | "createdAt" | "updatedAt">
export type UpdateRaceInput = Partial<CreateRaceInput>

export interface RacesFilters {
    search?: string
    status?: "all" | "active" | "inactive" | "all"
    page?: number
    limit?: number
}

export interface RacesListResponse {
    items: Race[]
    total: number
    page: number
    limit: number
}
```

```
1. /**
2.  * @fileoverview RacesProvider — seeds races from 5etools data.
3.  *
4.  * Reads: src/lib/5etools-data/races.json
5.  * Creates: Race documents via RaceModel
6.  *
7.  * Flow per item:
8.  *  1. Skip NPC-only races and reprinted (superseded) races
9.  *  2. Map speed, size, image, source
10.  *  3. Build HTML description from entries
11.  *  4. Call this.translateItem(name, description) — inherited from BaseProvider
12.  *  5. Collect matching subraces as variations (each translated separately)
13.  *  6. Check if race with that name already exists
14.  *  7. If not, create it
15.  */
16. 
17. import path from 'path';
18. import fs from 'fs';
19. import { BaseProvider, convertFeetToMeters } from '../base-provider';
20. import type { CreateRaceInput, RaceVariation, SizeCategory } from '../../../src/features/races/types/races.types';
21. import { RaceModel } from '../../../src/features/races/models/race';
22. import dbConnect from '../../../src/core/database/db';
23. 
24. const PROJECT_ROOT = path.resolve(__dirname, '../../../');
25. 
26. // ─── 5etools input types ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────
27. 
28. interface FiveEToolsEntry {
29.     type?: string;
30.     name?: string;
31.     entries?: (string | FiveEToolsEntry)[];
32.     items?: (string | FiveEToolsEntry)[];
33.     entry?: string;
34.     caption?: string;
35.     colLabels?: string[];
36.     rows?: unknown[][];
37. }
38. 
39. export interface FiveEToolsRace {
40.     name: string;
41.     source: string;
42.     page?: number;
43.     size?: string[];
44.     speed?: number | Record<string, number | boolean>;
45.     ability?: Record<string, number>[];
46.     age?: { mature?: number; max?: number };
47.     traitTags?: string[];
48.     languageProficiencies?: Record<string, boolean | number>[];
49.     darkvision?: number;
50.     resist?: (string | Record<string, unknown>)[];
51.     entries?: FiveEToolsEntry[];
52.     hasFluff?: boolean;
53.     hasFluffImages?: boolean;
54.     reprintedAs?: string[];
55.     lineage?: string;
56.     additionalSpells?: unknown[];
57.     soundClip?: unknown;

60. export interface FiveEToolsSubrace {
61.     name?: string;
62.     source: string;
63.     raceName: string;
64.     raceSource: string;
65.     page?: number;
66.     size?: string[];

69.     entries?: FiveEToolsEntry[];

71.     reprintedAs?: string[];
72.     _versions?: unknown[];

74. 
75. // ─── Helpers ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
76. 
77. const SIZE_MAP: Record<string, SizeCategory> = {
78.     S: 'Pequeno',
79.     M: 'Médio',
80.     L: 'Grande',
81. };
82. 
83. export function mapSize(sizeArr: string[] | undefined): SizeCategory {
84.     if (!sizeArr || sizeArr.length === 0) return 'Médio';
85.     for (const s of sizeArr) {
86.         const mapped = SIZE_MAP[s];
87.         if (mapped) return mapped;
88.     }
89.     return 'Médio';
90. }
91. 
92. function feetToMetersNum(feet: number): string {
93.     const m = feet * 0.3;
94.     return Number.isInteger(m) ? String(m) : m.toFixed(1).replace('.', ',');
95. }
96. 
97. const SPEED_LABELS: Record<string, string> = {
98.     walk: 'a pé',
99.     fly: 'voando',
100.     swim: 'nadando',
101.     climb: 'escalando',
102.     burrow: 'escavando',
103. };
104. 
105. export function mapSpeed(speed: number | Record<string, number | boolean> | undefined): string {
106.     if (speed === undefined) return '9 metros';
107. 
108.     if (typeof speed === 'number') {
109.         return `${feetToMetersNum(speed)} metros`;
110.     }
111. 
112.     const parts: string[] = [];
113.     for (const [key, value] of Object.entries(speed)) {
114.         const label = SPEED_LABELS[key] ?? key;
115.         if (typeof value === 'number') {
116.             parts.push(`${feetToMetersNum(value)} metros (${label})`);
117.         } else if (value === true) {
118.             // e.g. fly: true means "equal to walking speed"
119.             if (key === 'fly') {
120.                 parts.push('voo igual ao deslocamento a pé');
121.             } else {
122.                 parts.push(`deslocamento de ${label} igual ao deslocamento a pé`);
123.             }
124.         }
125.     }
126. 
127.     return parts.join(', ') || '9 metros';
128. }
129. 
130. function buildImageUrl(source: string, name: string): string {
131.     // 5etools image convention: https://5e.tools/img/{SOURCE}/{Name}.webp
132.     const encodedName = encodeURIComponent(name);
133.     return `https://5e.tools/img/${source}/${encodedName}.webp`;
134. }
135. 
136. function buildSourceLabel(source: string, page?: number): string {
137.     return page !== undefined ? `${source} pág. ${page}` : source;
138. }
139. 
140. /** Strip 5etools inline tag syntax from text before sending to AI. */
141. export function cleanText(text: string): string {
142.     return text
143.         .replace(/\{@damage\s+([^}]+)\}/g, '$1')
144.         .replace(/\{@scaledamage\s+([^|]+)\|[^|]+\|([^}]+)\}/g, '$2')
145.         .replace(/\{@dice\s+([^}]+)\}/g, '$1')
146.         .replace(/\{@hit\s+([^}]+)\}/g, '+$1')
147.         .replace(/\{@dc\s+([^}]+)\}/g, 'CD $1')
148.         .replace(/\{@[a-z]+\s+([^}|]+)(?:\|[^}]*)?\}/gi, '$1')
149.         .trim();
150. }
151. 
152. export function buildEntryHtml(entry: FiveEToolsEntry | string): string {
153.     if (typeof entry === 'string') {
154.         return `<p>${cleanText(entry)}</p>`;
155.     }
156. 
157.     const parts: string[] = [];
158. 
159.     if (entry.type === 'list' && Array.isArray(entry.items)) {
160.         const listItems = entry.items
161.             .map((item) => {
162.                 if (typeof item === 'string') return `<li>${cleanText(item)}</li>`;
163.                 const e = item as FiveEToolsEntry;
164.                 if (e.name && e.entry) {
165.                     return `<li><strong>${cleanText(e.name)}.</strong> ${cleanText(e.entry)}</li>`;
166.                 }
167.                 if (e.entry) return `<li>${cleanText(e.entry)}</li>`;
168.                 if (e.entries) return `<li>${(e.entries as string[]).map(cleanText).join(' ')}</li>`;
169.                 return '';
170.             })
171.             .filter(Boolean);
172.         parts.push(`<ul>${listItems.join('')}</ul>`);
173.     } else if (entry.type === 'table' && Array.isArray(entry.rows)) {
174.         // Skip complex tables in the seed description
175.     } else if (Array.isArray(entry.entries)) {
176.         const texts = entry.entries.map(buildEntryHtml).join('');
177.         if (entry.name) {
178.             parts.push(`<p><strong>${cleanText(entry.name)}.</strong></p>${texts}`);
179.         } else {
180.             parts.push(texts);
181.         }
182.     }
183. 
184.     return parts.join('');
185. }
186. 
187. export function buildDescriptionHtml(entries: FiveEToolsEntry[] | undefined): string {
188.     if (!entries || entries.length === 0) return '<p></p>';
189.     return entries.map(buildEntryHtml).join('');
190. }
191. 
192. // ─── RacesProvider ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
193. 
194. export class RacesProvider extends BaseProvider<FiveEToolsRace, CreateRaceInput> {
195.     readonly name = 'Races';
196.     readonly dataFilePath = 'src/lib/5etools-data/races.json';
197.     readonly dataKey = 'race';
198. 
199.     private subraces: FiveEToolsSubrace[] = [];
200. 
201.     override readDataFile(): FiveEToolsRace[] {
202.         const fullPath = path.resolve(PROJECT_ROOT, this.dataFilePath);
203.         const raw = fs.readFileSync(fullPath, 'utf-8');
204.         const parsed = JSON.parse(raw) as Record<string, unknown>;
205. 
206.         const races = parsed[this.dataKey];
207.         if (!Array.isArray(races)) {
208.             throw new Error(`Key "${this.dataKey}" not found or not an array in ${fullPath}`);
209.         }
210. 
211.         this.subraces = Array.isArray(parsed['subrace'])
212.             ? (parsed['subrace'] as FiveEToolsSubrace[])
213.             : [];
214. 
215.         this.log(`Loaded ${this.subraces.length} subraces`, 'dim');
216. 
217.         return races as FiveEToolsRace[];
218.     }
219. 
220.     async processItem(race: FiveEToolsRace): Promise<CreateRaceInput | null> {
221.         // Skip NPC-only races
222.         if (race.traitTags?.includes('NPC Race')) {
223.             this.log(`Skipping NPC race: ${race.name} (${race.source})`, 'dim');
224.             return null;
225.         }
226. 
227.         // Skip races superseded by a newer printing
228.         if (race.reprintedAs && race.reprintedAs.length > 0) {
229.             this.log(`Skipping reprinted race: ${race.name} (${race.source}) → ${race.reprintedAs[0]}`, 'dim');
230.             return null;
231.         }
232. 
233.         // Build description HTML and translate
234.         const descriptionHtml = buildDescriptionHtml(race.entries);
235.         const { name, description } = await this.translateItem(race.name, descriptionHtml);
236. 
237.         // Map variations (subraces)
238.         const matchingSubraces = this.subraces.filter(
239.             (sr) => sr.raceName === race.name && sr.raceSource === race.source,
240.         );
241. 
242.         const variations: RaceVariation[] = [];
243.         for (const subrace of matchingSubraces) {
244.             // Skip reprinted subraces
245.             if (subrace.reprintedAs && subrace.reprintedAs.length > 0) continue;
246. 
247.             const subraceDescHtml = buildDescriptionHtml(subrace.entries);
248.             const subraceNameRaw = subrace.name ?? race.name;
249. 
250.             const { name: subraceName, description: subraceDescription } =
251.                 await this.translateItem(subraceNameRaw, subraceDescHtml);
252. 
253.             variations.push({
254.                 name: subraceName,
255.                 description: subraceDescription,
256.                 source: buildSourceLabel(subrace.source, subrace.page),
257.                 image: subrace.hasFluffImages
258.                     ? buildImageUrl(subrace.source, subraceNameRaw)
259.                     : '',
260.                 traits: [],
261.                 spells: [],
262.                 size: mapSize(subrace.size),
263.                 speed: subrace.speed ? mapSpeed(subrace.speed) : undefined,
264.             });
265.         }
266. 
267.         return {
268.             name,
269.             description: convertFeetToMeters(description),
270.             source: buildSourceLabel(race.source, race.page),
271.             status: 'active',
272.             size: mapSize(race.size),
273.             speed: mapSpeed(race.speed),
274.             image: race.hasFluffImages ? buildImageUrl(race.source, race.name) : '',
275.             traits: [],
276.             spells: [],
277.             variations,
278.         };
279.     }
280. 
281.     async findExisting(race: CreateRaceInput): Promise<CreateRaceInput | null> {
282.         await dbConnect();
283.         const doc = await RaceModel.findOne({ name: race.name }).lean();
284.         if (!doc) return null;
285. 
286.         return {
287.             name: doc.name,
288.             description: doc.description,
289.             source: doc.source,
290.             status: doc.status,
291.             size: doc.size,
292.             speed: doc.speed,
293.             image: doc.image ?? '',
294.             traits: doc.traits.map((t) => ({
295.                 name: t.name,
296.                 description: t.description,
297.                 level: t.level,
298.             })),
299.             spells: doc.spells,
300.             variations: doc.variations.map((v) => ({
301.                 name: v.name,
302.                 description: v.description,
303.                 source: v.source,
304.                 image: v.image ?? '',
305.                 color: v.color,
306.                 traits: v.traits.map((t) => ({
307.                     name: t.name,
308.                     description: t.description,
309.                     level: t.level,
310.                 })),
311.                 spells: v.spells,
312.                 size: v.size,
313.                 speed: v.speed,
314.             })),
315.         };
316.     }
317. 
318.     async create(race: CreateRaceInput): Promise<void> {
319.         await dbConnect();
320.         await RaceModel.create(race);
321.     }
322. 
323.     async update(race: CreateRaceInput): Promise<void> {
324.         await dbConnect();
325.         await RaceModel.findOneAndUpdate(
326.             { name: race.name },
327.             { $set: race },
328.             { runValidators: true },
329.         );
330.     }
331. 
332.     override getItemLabel(item: CreateRaceInput): string {
333.         return item.name;
334.     }
335. }
336.
```

```
388.             printColoredJson(current);
389.             term('\n');
390.             term.bold('────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────\n');
391. 
392.             if (isDryRun) {
393.                 term.yellow('  (modo dry-run — não será salvo no banco)\n');
394.             }
395. 
396.             term('\n');
397.             term.cyan('Glossário ');
398.             term.gray('(formato: "termo > tradução ; outro > outro" — vazio para confirmar)');
399.             term.cyan(': ');
400. 
401.             const input = await new Promise<string>((resolve) => {
402.                 term.inputField({}, (_, value) => {
403.                     term('\n');
404.                     resolve((value ?? '').trim());
405.                 });
406.             });
407. 
408.             // Empty input = confirm
409.             if (!input) {
410.                 return current;
411.             }
412. 
413.             // Parse and validate
414.             const { entries: newEntries, errors } = parseGlossaryInput(input);
415. 
416.             if (errors.length > 0) {
417.                 for (const err of errors) {
418.                     term.red(`  ✗ ${err}\n`);
419.                 }
420.                 term.yellow('  Por favor, corrija o formato e tente novamente.\n');
421.                 continue;
422.             }
423. 
424.             if (newEntries.length === 0) {
425.                 term.yellow('  Nenhuma entrada reconhecida. Tente novamente.\n');
426.                 continue;
427.             }
428. 
429.             // Save new entries to MongoDB
430.             await saveEntries(newEntries);
431.             term.green(`  ✓ ${newEntries.length} entrada(s) salva(s) no glossário.\n`);
432. 
433.             // Reload and reapply all entries (including newly saved ones)
434.             entries = await loadAllEntries();
435.             current = this.applyGlossaryToOutput(output, entries);
436.         }
437.     }
438. 
439.     // ─── Main loop ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
440. 
441.     async run(): Promise<void> {
442.         this.log(`\nStarting provider: ${this.name}`, 'info');
443. 
444.         const items = this.readDataFile();
445.         const startIndex = this.testMode ? 0 : (await this.readProgress()) + 1;
446. 
447.         this.log(`Total items: ${items.length}`, 'dim');
448. 
449.         if (!this.testMode && startIndex >= items.length) {
450.             this.log(`All ${items.length} items already processed. Use --reset-progress to restart.`, 'warn');
451.             return;
452.         }
453. 
454.         if (this.testMode) {
455.             this.log(`\n🧪 TEST MODE: Finding first processable item...`, 'info');
456.             const limit = Math.min(items.length, 20);
457.             for (let i = 0; i < limit; i++) {
458.                 const result = await this.runInteractiveItem(items[i], i, true);
459.                 if (result !== 'skipped') break;
460.                 this.log(`  Item ${i} skipped — trying next...`, 'dim');
461.             }
462.             return;
463.         }
464. 
465.         if (this.autoMode) {
466.             await this.runAutoLoop(items, startIndex);
467.         } else {
468.             await this.runInteractiveLoop(items, startIndex);
469.         }
470.     }
471. 
472.     // ─── Auto mode (batch, no confirmation) ──────────────────────────────────
473. 
474.     private async runAutoLoop(items: TInput[], startIndex: number): Promise<void> {
475.         this.log(
476.             startIndex > 0
477.                 ? `Resuming from index ${startIndex} (${items.length - startIndex} remaining)`
478.                 : `Starting from the beginning`,
479.             'dim'
480.         );
481. 
482.         this.initProgressBar(items.length, startIndex);
483. 
484.         // Load glossary once for the full run
485.         const entries = await loadAllEntries();
486.         if (entries.length > 0) {
487.             this.log(`Glossário carregado: ${entries.length} entrada(s)`, 'dim');
488.         }
489. 
490.         let created = 0;
491.         let skipped = 0;
492. 
493.         for (let i = startIndex; i < items.length; i++) {
494.             const item = items[i];
495. 
496.             try {
497.                 const raw = await this.processItem(item);
498. 
499.                 if (raw === null) {
500.                     this.log(`[${i}] Skipped (processItem returned null)`, 'dim');
```

/home/burgos/code/dndicas/scripts/seed-data/base-provider.ts (lines 590-660)

<details>
<summary>71 lines</summary>

```
590.     private async runInteractiveItem(
591.         item: TInput,
592.         index: number,
593.         isDryRun: boolean,
594.     ): Promise<'created' | 'updated' | 'skipped' | 'exists'> {
595.         const raw = await this.processItem(item);
596. 
597.         if (raw === null) {
598.             term.yellow('  ⚠  Item ignorado (processItem retornou null)\n');
599.             if (!isDryRun) await this.saveProgress(index);
600.             return 'skipped';
601.         }
602. 
603.         // Apply glossary silently so findExisting uses the canonicalized name
604.         // (a previous run may have stored the item with the glossary applied,
605.         // so searching with the raw AI-translated name could miss it)
606.         const glossaryEntries = await loadAllEntries();
607.         const glossarized = this.applyGlossaryToOutput(raw, glossaryEntries);
608. 
609.         // Resolve conflicts field by field BEFORE the glossary review step
610.         const existing = await this.findExisting(glossarized);
611.         let working: TOutput = glossarized;
612. 
613.         if (existing) {
614.             const diffs = this.diffObjects(existing, glossarized);
615.             if (diffs.length > 0) {
616.                 working = await this.resolveConflictsFieldByField(existing, glossarized, diffs);
617.             } else if (!isDryRun) {
618.                 term.yellow('  ⚠  Já existe no banco e está igual — ignorando.\n');
619.                 await this.saveProgress(index);
620.                 return 'exists';
621.             }
622.         }
623. 
624.         // Interactive review: show result, allow glossary corrections
625.         const final = await this.reviewAndConfirmItem(working, isDryRun);
626. 
627.         if (isDryRun) {
628.             term.green('\n✓ Modo dry-run — nenhum dado foi salvo.\n');
629.             return 'skipped';
630.         }
631. 
632.         if (existing) {
633.             const finalDiffs = this.diffObjects(existing, final);
634.             if (finalDiffs.length === 0) {
635.                 term.yellow('  ⚠  Resultado igual ao existente — ignorando.\n');
636.                 await this.saveProgress(index);
637.                 return 'exists';
638.             }
639.             await this.update(final);
640.             term.green('  ✓ Atualizado com sucesso.\n');
641.             await this.saveProgress(index);
642.             return 'updated';
643.         }
644. 
645.         await this.create(final);
646.         term.green(`  ✓ Criado com sucesso.\n`);
647.         await this.saveProgress(index);
648.         return 'created';
649.     }
650. 
651.     // ─── Abstract methods ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────
652. 
653.     /**
654.      * Map and translate a single 5etools item into the system input format.
655.      * Return null to skip the item entirely.
656.      */
657.     abstract processItem(item: TInput): Promise<TOutput | null>;
658. 
659.     /**
660.      * Find an existing item in the database that matches the incoming item.
```

```
97.         expect(mapSize(undefined)).toBe('Médio');
98.     });
99. 
100.     it('returns "Médio" for empty array', () => {
101.         expect(mapSize([])).toBe('Médio');
102.     });
103. 
104.     it('maps M to "Médio"', () => {
105.         expect(mapSize(['M'])).toBe('Médio');
106.     });
107. 
108.     it('maps S to "Pequeno"', () => {
109.         expect(mapSize(['S'])).toBe('Pequeno');
110.     });
111. 
112.     it('maps L to "Grande"', () => {
113.         expect(mapSize(['L'])).toBe('Grande');
114.     });
115. 
116.     it('returns first mappable size when array has multiple entries', () => {
117.         expect(mapSize(['S', 'M'])).toBe('Pequeno');
118.     });
119. 
120.     it('falls back to "Médio" for unknown size codes', () => {
121.         expect(mapSize(['X', 'T'])).toBe('Médio');
122.     });
123. });
124. 
125. // ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
126. // mapSpeed
127. // ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
128. 
129. describe('mapSpeed', () => {
130.     it('returns "9 metros" for undefined', () => {
131.         expect(mapSpeed(undefined)).toBe('9 metros');
132.     });
133. 
134.     it('converts 30 feet to "9 metros"', () => {
135.         expect(mapSpeed(30)).toBe('9 metros');
136.     });
137. 
138.     it('converts 25 feet to "7,5 metros"', () => {
139.         expect(mapSpeed(25)).toBe('7,5 metros');
140.     });
141. 
142.     it('formats walk + fly object with numeric fly speed', () => {
143.         expect(mapSpeed({ walk: 30, fly: 50 })).toBe('9 metros (a pé), 15 metros (voando)');
144.     });
145. 
146.     it('handles fly: true as "voo igual ao deslocamento a pé"', () => {
147.         expect(mapSpeed({ walk: 30, fly: true })).toBe('9 metros (a pé), voo igual ao deslocamento a pé');
148.     });
149. 
150.     it('formats walk + swim correctly', () => {
151.         expect(mapSpeed({ walk: 25, swim: 25 })).toBe('7,5 metros (a pé), 7,5 metros (nadando)');
152.     });
153. 
154.     it('formats climb speed', () => {
155.         const result = mapSpeed({ walk: 30, climb: 30 });
156.         expect(result).toContain('escalando');
157.     });
158. 
159.     it('returns "9 metros" for empty speed object', () => {
160.         expect(mapSpeed({})).toBe('9 metros');
161.     });
162. });
163. 
164. // ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
165. // cleanText
166. // ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
167. 
168. describe('cleanText', () => {
169.     it('strips {@damage} tags', () => {
170.         expect(cleanText('deals {@damage 1d6} damage')).toBe('deals 1d6 damage');
171.     });
172. 
173.     it('strips {@spell} tags', () => {
174.         expect(cleanText('cast {@spell fireball}')).toBe('cast fireball');
175.     });
176. 
177.     it('strips {@condition} tags', () => {
178.         expect(cleanText('becomes {@condition frightened}')).toBe('becomes frightened');
179.     });
180. 
181.     it('converts {@dc} to "CD"', () => {
182.         expect(cleanText('DC {@dc 8}')).toBe('DC CD 8');
183.     });
184. 
185.     it('strips {@hit} tags with + prefix', () => {
186.         expect(cleanText('make a {@hit 5} attack')).toBe('make a +5 attack');
187.     });
188. 
189.     it('handles tags with pipe separators', () => {
190.         expect(cleanText('{@spell gust of wind|XPHB}')).toBe('gust of wind');
191.     });
192. 
193.     it('returns plain text unchanged', () => {
194.         expect(cleanText('You gain darkvision.')).toBe('You gain darkvision.');
195.     });
196. });
197. 
198. // ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

203.     it('returns "<p></p>" for undefined', () => {
204.         expect(buildDescriptionHtml(undefined)).toBe('<p></p>');
205.     });
206. 
207.     it('returns "<p></p>" for empty array', () => {
208.         expect(buildDescriptionHtml([])).toBe('<p></p>');
209.     });
210. });

212. describe('buildEntryHtml', () => {
213.     it('wraps a plain string in <p>', () => {

215.     });
216.

218.         const entry = {

220.             name: 'Darkvision',
221.             entries: ['You can see in dim light.'],
222.         };

224.         expect(html).toContain('<strong>Darkvision.</strong>');
225.         expect(html).toContain('You can see in dim light.');
226.     });
227. 
228.     it('renders list entries as <ul><li>', () => {
229.         const entry = {
230.             type: 'list',
231.             items: ['Item one', 'Item two'],
232.         };
233.         const html = buildEntryHtml(entry);
234.         expect(html).toContain('<ul>');
235.         expect(html).toContain('<li>Item one</li>');
236.         expect(html).toContain('<li>Item two</li>');
237.     });
238. 
239.     it('renders list items with name+entry as bold name', () => {
240.         const entry = {

242.             items: [{ name: 'Acid', entry: 'Deals acid damage.' }],
243.         };
244.         const html = buildEntryHtml(entry);
245.         expect(html).toContain('<strong>Acid.</strong>');
246.         expect(html).toContain('Deals acid damage.');
247.     });
248. 
249.     it('skips table entries without crashing', () => {
250.         const entry = { type: 'table', rows: [[1, 2]] };
251.         expect(() => buildEntryHtml(entry)).not.toThrow();
252.     });
253. 
254.     it('strips 5etools tags in entry text', () => {
255.         const html = buildEntryHtml('You deal {@damage 1d4} slashing.');
256.         expect(html).toContain('1d4');
257.         expect(html).not.toContain('{@');
258.     });
259. });
```

<sub>⏱️ 92m 43s</sub>

### 💬 Copilot

All errors are pre-existing in `search-cache/` — none in our files. The implementation is complete.

Here's a summary of what was implemented:

**`base-provider.ts`** — Added `afterReview(output, isDryRun)` hook:
- Called between glossary review and save steps
- Default no-op; providers override to run post-review logic

**`races-provider.ts`** — Major refactor:
- Loads `fluff-races.json` in `readDataFile()` into a keyed Map
- **Description**: sourced from fluff lore entries (not mechanical entries)
- **Image**: sourced from `fluff.images[0].href.path` → `https://5e.tools/img/{path}` (or external URL)
- **Traits**: `extractTraits()` maps named `race.entries[]` to `RaceTrait[]`, each with translated name + description; subraces get their own traits too
- **`afterReview()` override**: calls `resolveTraits()` for the race and each variation
- **`resolveTraits()`**: for each trait, searches the `Trait` collection by name; if none found → creates it; if found → shows a `singleColumnMenu` with formatted options (create new `"Name (RaceName)"` or use existing), then updates the `_id` on the embedded trait

**Tests** — 47 tests all passing:
- Updated `buildDescriptionHtml` tests (now returns `''` for empty)
- New `extractTraits` suite (6 tests)
- Updated `processItem` suite: traits from entries, fluff description/image, variation traits
- Added `Trait` model mock + `singleColumnMenu` to terminal-kit mock

```
351.     private applyGlossaryToOutput(output: TOutput, entries: GlossaryEntry[]): TOutput {
352.         if (!entries.length) return output;
353.         const obj = output as Record<string, unknown>;
354.         const result = { ...obj };
355. 
356.         if (typeof result['name'] === 'string') {
357.             result['name'] = applyGlossary(entries, result['name']);
358.         }
359.         if (typeof result['description'] === 'string') {
360.             result['description'] = applyGlossary(entries, result['description']);
361.         }
362. 
363.         return result as TOutput;
364.     }
```

### 💬 Copilot

The fix is clear: `applyGlossaryToOutput` only touches `name` and `description` at the top level, ignoring traits. I'll make the method `protected` and override it in `RacesProvider` to also apply the glossary to trait names/descriptions and inside variations.

<sub>⏱️ 99m 35s</sub>

### 💬 Copilot

All 47 tests pass. The fix:

- Changed `applyGlossaryToOutput` from `private` → `protected` in `base-provider.ts`
- Added an override in `RacesProvider` that calls `super.applyGlossaryToOutput()` (handles race `name` + `description`), then also applies the glossary to:
  - Each trait's `name` and `description`
  - Each variation's `name` and `description`
  - Each variation's traits' `name` and `description`

Now when you enter `"Talons. \> Garras"` in the glossary prompt, it will replace "Talons." everywhere — including trait names.

### ✓ Task Complete

Fixed glossary not applying to trait names/descriptions. The `applyGlossaryToOutput` method in `base-provider.ts` was `private` and only applied glossary to the top-level `name` and `description` fields. Changes made:

1. **`base-provider.ts`**: Changed `applyGlossaryToOutput` from `private` to `protected` to allow overriding.
2. **`races-provider.ts`**: Added `applyGlossaryToOutput` override that calls `super` then additionally applies the glossary to all trait `name`/`description` fields and all variation `name`/`description`/`traits` fields.

All 47 tests still pass.

```
54. export interface DiffEntry {
55.     field: string;
56.     oldValue: unknown;
57.     newValue: unknown;
58. }
59. 
60. function formatValue(v: unknown): string {
61.     if (v === undefined) return '(não definido)';
62.     if (v === null) return '(nulo)';
63.     if (typeof v === 'string') return v;
64.     return JSON.stringify(v);
65. }
66. 
67. function truncateStr(s: string, maxLen = 120): string {
68.     return s.length > maxLen ? s.slice(0, maxLen - 3) + '...' : s;
69. }
70. 
71. // ─── Colored JSON printer ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────
72. 
73. /**
74.  * Prints a syntax-highlighted JSON representation of `obj` to the terminal.
75.  *
76.  * Color scheme:
77.  *   - Keys        → yellow
78.  *   - Strings     → green
79.  *   - Numbers     → cyan
80.  *   - Booleans    → blue
81.  *   - null        → gray
82.  *   - Brackets    → bold white
83.  *   - Punctuation → default
84.  */
85. function printColoredJson(obj: unknown): void {
86.     const str = JSON.stringify(obj, null, 2);
87.     // Tokenize: quoted strings (optionally followed by ": "), numbers,
88.     // keywords, brackets, punctuation, and whitespace.
89.     const re = /("(?:[^"\\]|\\.)*")(\s*:)?|true|false|null|-?\d+(?:\.\d+)?(?:[eE][+-]?\d+)?|[{}\[\],:]|\n|[^\S\n]+/g;
90. 
91.     let m: RegExpExecArray | null;
92.     while ((m = re.exec(str)) !== null) {
93.         const tok = m[0];
94.         const quotedStr = m[1];
95.         const colonSuffix = m[2];
96. 
97.         if (quotedStr !== undefined) {
98.             if (colonSuffix !== undefined) {
99.                 term.yellow(quotedStr);
100.                 term(colonSuffix);
101.             } else {
102.                 term.cyan(quotedStr);
103.             }
104.         } else if (tok === 'true' || tok === 'false') {
105.             term.blue(tok);
106.         } else if (tok === 'null') {
107.             term.gray(tok);
108.         } else if (tok === '{' || tok === '}' || tok === '[' || tok === ']') {
109.             term.bold.white(tok);
110.         } else if (/^-?\d/.test(tok)) {
111.             term.green(tok);
112.         } else {
113.             term(tok);
114.         }
115.     }
116. }
117. 
118. const PROJECT_ROOT = path.resolve(__dirname, '../../');
119. 
120. // ─── Unit conversion ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
121. 
122. /**
123.  * Converts any "X pés", "X feet", "X foot" or "X ft" occurrences in a text
124.  * to meters using the D&D standard (5 ft = 1.5 m, i.e. × 0.3).
125.  * Also converts "X mile(s)" to km (1 mile = 1.5 km by the same standard).
126.  */
127. export function convertFeetToMeters(text: string): string {
128.     return text
```

```
278.     private diffObjects(existing: TOutput, incoming: TOutput): DiffEntry[] {
279.         const a = existing as Record<string, unknown>;
280.         const b = incoming as Record<string, unknown>;
281.         const allFields = new Set([...Object.keys(a), ...Object.keys(b)]);
282.         const diffs: DiffEntry[] = [];
283.         for (const field of allFields) {
284.             const normA = this.normalizeForDiff(a[field]);
285.             const normB = this.normalizeForDiff(b[field]);
286.             if (JSON.stringify(normA) !== JSON.stringify(normB)) {
287.                 diffs.push({ field, oldValue: a[field], newValue: b[field] });
288.             }
289.         }
290.         return diffs;
291.     }
292. 
293.     /**
294.      * Shows each conflicting field individually and lets the user decide
295.      * field by field whether to keep the existing value (←) or use the
296.      * incoming one (→). Works identically in dry-run and live mode.
297.      *
298.      * @returns A merged TOutput built from existing + chosen incoming fields.
299.      */
300.     private async resolveConflictsFieldByField(
301.         existing: TOutput,
302.         incoming: TOutput,
303.         diffs: DiffEntry[],
304.     ): Promise<TOutput> {
305.         const label = this.getItemLabel(incoming);
306.         term('\n');
307.         term.bold(`─── Conflito: ${label} ─────────────────────────────────────────\n`);
308.         term.yellow(`  ${diffs.length} campo(s) diferente(s) — resolva cada um:\n\n`);
309. 
310.         const result = { ...(existing as Record<string, unknown>) };
311. 
312.         for (const diff of diffs) {
313.             term.bold(`  ${diff.field}:\n`);
314.             term.red(`    ← ${truncateStr(formatValue(diff.oldValue))}  (existente)\n`);
315.             term.green(`    → ${truncateStr(formatValue(diff.newValue))}  (novo)\n`);
316.             term.bold('  ← seta esquerda: manter existente  |  → seta direita: usar novo\n');
317. 
318.             const choice = await new Promise<'keep' | 'update'>((resolve) => {
319.                 term.grabInput(true);
320.                 const handler = (name: string) => {
321.                     if (name === 'CTRL_C') { term.grabInput(false); process.exit(0); }
322.                     if (name === 'LEFT') {
323.                         term.grabInput(false);
324.                         term.removeListener('key', handler);
325.                         term.yellow('  ← Mantendo existente.\n\n');
326.                         resolve('keep');
327.                     } else if (name === 'RIGHT') {
328.                         term.grabInput(false);
329.                         term.removeListener('key', handler);
330.                         term.green('  → Usando novo.\n\n');
331.                         resolve('update');
332.                     }
333.                 };
334.                 term.on('key', handler);
335.             });
336. 
337.             if (choice === 'update') {
338.                 result[diff.field] = diff.newValue;
339.             }
340.         }
341. 
342.         return result as TOutput;
343.     }
344. 
345. 
346. 
347.     /**
348.      * Applies the current glossary to all string fields of an output object.
349.      * Only processes `name` and `description` fields (both are translatable text).
350.      */
```

```
271.     private normalizeForDiff(v: unknown): unknown {
272.         if (v === null) return undefined;
273.         if (v === '') return undefined;
274.         if (Array.isArray(v) && v.length === 0) return undefined;
275.         return v;
276.     }
277. 
278.     private diffObjects(existing: TOutput, incoming: TOutput): DiffEntry[] {
279.         const a = existing as Record<string, unknown>;
280.         const b = incoming as Record<string, unknown>;
281.         const allFields = new Set([...Object.keys(a), ...Object.keys(b)]);
282.         const diffs: DiffEntry[] = [];
283.         for (const field of allFields) {
284.             const normA = this.normalizeForDiff(a[field]);
285.             const normB = this.normalizeForDiff(b[field]);
286.             if (JSON.stringify(normA) !== JSON.stringify(normB)) {
287.                 diffs.push({ field, oldValue: a[field], newValue: b[field] });
288.             }
289.         }
290.         return diffs;
291.     }
292.
```

</details>

<sub>⏱️ 108m 57s</sub>

### 💬 Copilot

The implementation is structurally correct — both `findExisting` and `update` are present. But I notice a real issue: `findExisting` strips `_id` from traits in the mapped result, while `afterReview` adds new `_id`s. This means `diffObjects(existing, final)` will always find traits as different (because `final` has `_id` on each trait but `existing` doesn't), making `update` always fire. Let me verify this and also check that the `normalizeForDiff` handles the `_id` field properly:

<sub>⏱️ 110m 13s</sub>

### 💬 Copilot

Found two real issues:

1. **Trait `_id` stripped in `findExisting`** — after first run, DB stores trait with `_id` (Trait collection ref), but `findExisting` strips it. On second run, `diffObjects(existing, final)` always sees traits as different because `final` has `_id` but `existing` doesn't → `update` fires every time unnecessarily.

2. **`level` mismatch** — `extractTraits` returns traits without `level`, but DB default is `1`. So `existing.traits[i].level = 1` while `final.traits[i].level = undefined` → also always triggers a spurious diff.

Both issues cause the conflict resolver to always show traits as changed even when nothing really changed. Fix:

---

<sub>⏱️ 110m 49s</sub>

### 💬 Copilot

All 47 tests pass. Here's a summary of what was fixed and verified:

**Two bugs fixed that were breaking the conflict resolver for races:**

1. **`extractTraits` missing `level: 1`** — traits returned from `processItem` had no `level`, but the DB stores `level: 1` by default. When `findExisting` read them back with `level: 1`, `diffObjects` always saw traits as different even if nothing changed. Fixed by adding `level: 1` to `extractTraits` so both sides match.

2. **`findExisting` stripping `_id` from traits** — after the first run, each trait in the DB has an `_id` pointing to the Trait collection document. On subsequent runs, `afterReview` resolves the same trait by name and gets the same `_id`, but `findExisting` was discarding it — so `diffObjects(existing, final)` always found differences. Fixed by including `_id: t._id ? String(t._id) : undefined` in both the base race traits and variation traits mappings.

**The conflict resolver was already correctly wired up** (both `findExisting` and `update` were present), just the above mismatches were causing spurious diffs on every re-run.

---

<sub>⏱️ 111m 5s</sub>

### ✓ Task Complete

Fixed conflict resolver for races provider. Two bugs were causing the resolver to always show traits as different even when nothing changed:

1. **`extractTraits` missing `level: 1`** — `processItem` returned traits without `level`, but DB stores `level: 1` by default. On re-runs, `diffObjects` always detected a diff. Fixed by adding `level: 1` in `extractTraits`.

2. **`findExisting` stripping trait `_id`** — After first run, each race trait's `_id` stores the Trait collection reference. But `findExisting` was discarding it, so `diffObjects(existing, final)` always found differences. Fixed by including `_id: t._id ? String(t._id) : undefined` in both race-level and variation-level trait mappings.

The pattern now mirrors the spells provider: `findExisting` + `update` are correctly implemented, and the data shapes from `processItem`/`afterReview` match what `findExisting` returns — so the conflict resolver only fires when data truly changed.

All 47 tests pass.

```
300.     private async resolveConflictsFieldByField(
301.         existing: TOutput,
302.         incoming: TOutput,
303.         diffs: DiffEntry[],
304.     ): Promise<TOutput> {
305.         const label = this.getItemLabel(incoming);
306.         term('\n');
307.         term.bold(`─── Conflito: ${label} ─────────────────────────────────────────\n`);
308.         term.yellow(`  ${diffs.length} campo(s) diferente(s) — resolva cada um:\n\n`);
309. 
310.         const result = { ...(existing as Record<string, unknown>) };
311. 
312.         for (const diff of diffs) {
313.             term.bold(`  ${diff.field}:\n`);
314.             term.red(`    ← ${truncateStr(formatValue(diff.oldValue))}  (existente)\n`);
315.             term.green(`    → ${truncateStr(formatValue(diff.newValue))}  (novo)\n`);
316.             term.bold('  ← seta esquerda: manter existente  |  → seta direita: usar novo\n');
317. 
318.             const choice = await new Promise<'keep' | 'update'>((resolve) => {
319.                 term.grabInput(true);
320.                 const handler = (name: string) => {
321.                     if (name === 'CTRL_C') { term.grabInput(false); process.exit(0); }
322.                     if (name === 'LEFT') {
323.                         term.grabInput(false);
324.                         term.removeListener('key', handler);
325.                         term.yellow('  ← Mantendo existente.\n\n');
326.                         resolve('keep');
327.                     } else if (name === 'RIGHT') {
328.                         term.grabInput(false);
329.                         term.removeListener('key', handler);
330.                         term.green('  → Usando novo.\n\n');
331.                         resolve('update');
332.                     }
333.                 };
334.                 term.on('key', handler);
335.             });
336. 
337.             if (choice === 'update') {
338.                 result[diff.field] = diff.newValue;
339.             }
340.         }
341. 
342.         return result as TOutput;
343.     }
344. 
345.
```

</details>

<sub>⏱️ 156m 40s</sub>

### ✅ `view`

**view the file at /home/burgos/code/dndicas/scripts/seed-data/base-provider.ts.**

/home/burgos/code/dndicas/scripts/seed-data/base-provider.ts (lines 1-100)

<details>
<summary>100 lines</summary>

```
1. /**
2.  * @fileoverview Abstract base class for all seed data providers.
3.  *
4.  * Each provider reads a 5etools JSON file, translates items via a pluggable
5.  * translator, checks for duplicates, and creates records in the system.
6.  *
7.  * Usage:
8.  *   class MyProvider extends BaseProvider<TInput, TOutput> { ... }
9.  *
10.  * ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
11.  * IMAGENS DO 5ETOOLS
12.  * ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
13.  * Os JSONs do 5etools NÃO contêm URLs de imagem diretamente. Em vez disso,
14.  * usam a flag booleana `hasFluffImages: true` para indicar que existe imagem
15.  * disponível externamente.
16.  *
17.  * Para exibir a imagem na UI, buscar via:
18.  *   https://5e.tools/img/{source}/{name}.webp
19.  *   (ex: https://5e.tools/img/MPMM/Aarakocra.webp)
20.  *
21.  * Cobertura por tipo de entidade:
22.  *   - Classes  : ~93% têm imagem (14 de 15 classes)
23.  *   - Raças    : ~84% têm imagem (133 de 158 raças)
24.  *   - Itens    : ~31% têm imagem (764 de 2451 itens)
25.  *   - Base items: ~28% têm imagem (55 de 196 itens)
26.  *   - Feats    : ~11% têm imagem (29 de 265 feats)
27.  *   - Spells   : ~3%  têm imagem (12 de 361 spells)
28.  *
29.  * Ao implementar, verificar `hasFluffImages === true` antes de tentar
30.  * carregar a imagem para evitar requisições desnecessárias.
31.  * ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
32.  */
33. 
34. import fs from 'fs';
35. import path from 'path';

60. function formatValue(v: unknown): string {
61.     if (v === undefined) return '(não definido)';
62.     if (v === null) return '(nulo)';
63.     if (typeof v === 'string') return v;

67. function truncateStr(s: string, maxLen = 120): string {
68.     return s.length > maxLen ? s.slice(0, maxLen - 3) + '...' : s;
69. }

71. // ─── Colored JSON printer ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────

73. /**
74.  * Prints a syntax-highlighted JSON representation of `obj` to the terminal.
75.  *
76.  * Color scheme:
77.  *   - Keys        → yellow
78.  *   - Strings     → green
79.  *   - Numbers     → cyan
80.  *   - Booleans    → blue
81.  *   - null        → gray
82.  *   - Brackets    → bold white
83.  *   - Punctuation → default
84.  */
85. function printColoredJson(obj: unknown): void {
86.     const str = JSON.stringify(obj, null, 2);
87.     // Tokenize: quoted strings (optionally followed by ": "), numbers,
88.     // keywords, brackets, punctuation, and whitespace.
89.     const re = /("(?:[^"\\]|\\.)*")(\s*:)?|true|false|null|-?\d+(?:\.\d+)?(?:[eE][+-]?\d+)?|[{}\[\],:]|\n|[^\S\n]+/g;
90. 
91.     let m: RegExpExecArray | null;
92.     while ((m = re.exec(str)) !== null) {
93.         const tok = m[0];
94.         const quotedStr = m[1];
95.         const colonSuffix = m[2];
96. 
97.         if (quotedStr !== undefined) {
98.             if (colonSuffix !== undefined) {
99.                 term.yellow(quotedStr);
```

```
122. /**
123.  * Converts any "X pés", "X feet", "X foot" or "X ft" occurrences in a text
124.  * to meters using the D&D standard (5 ft = 1.5 m, i.e. × 0.3).
125.  * Also converts "X mile(s)" to km (1 mile = 1.5 km by the same standard).
126.  */
127. export function convertFeetToMeters(text: string): string {
128.     return text
129.         .replace(/(\d+(?:[.,]\d+)?)\s*(?:pés?|feet|foot|ft\.?)/gi, (_, numStr: string) => {
130.             const feet = parseFloat(numStr.replace(',', '.'));
131.             const meters = feet * 0.3;
132.             const formatted = Number.isInteger(meters)
133.                 ? String(meters)
134.                 : meters.toFixed(1).replace('.', ',');
135.             return `${formatted} metros`;
136.         })
137.         .replace(/(\d+(?:[.,]\d+)?)\s*(?:milhas?|miles?)/gi, (_, numStr: string) => {
138.             const miles = parseFloat(numStr.replace(',', '.'));
139.             const km = miles * 1.5;
140.             const formatted = Number.isInteger(km)
141.                 ? String(km)
142.                 : km.toFixed(1).replace('.', ',');
143.             return `${formatted} km`;
144.         });
145. }

196.         }
```

```
295.      * field by field whether to keep the existing value (←) or use the

297.      *

299.      */

315.             term.green(`    → ${truncateStr(formatValue(diff.newValue))}  (novo)\n`);
316.             term.bold('  ← seta esquerda: manter existente  |  → seta direita: usar novo\n');

318.             const choice = await new Promise<'keep' | 'update'>((resolve) => {
319.                 term.grabInput(true);
320.                 const handler = (name: string) => {
321.                     if (name === 'CTRL_C') { term.grabInput(false); process.exit(0); }
322.                     if (name === 'LEFT') {
323.                         term.grabInput(false);
324.                         term.removeListener('key', handler);
325.                         term.yellow('  ← Mantendo existente.\n\n');
326.                         resolve('keep');
327.                     } else if (name === 'RIGHT') {
328.                         term.grabInput(false);
329.                         term.removeListener('key', handler);
330.                         term.green('  → Usando novo.\n\n');
331.                         resolve('update');
332.                     }
333.                 };
334.                 term.on('key', handler);
335.             });
336. 
337.             if (choice === 'update') {
338.                 result[diff.field] = diff.newValue;
339.             }
340.         }
341. 
342.         return result as TOutput;
343.     }
```

```
381.     private async reviewAndConfirmItem(
382.         output: TOutput,
383.         isDryRun: boolean,
384.     ): Promise<TOutput> {
385.         let entries = await loadAllEntries();
386.         let current = this.applyGlossaryToOutput(output, entries);
387. 
388.         // eslint-disable-next-line no-constant-condition
389.         while (true) {
390.             // Display current state
391.             term('\n');
392.             term.bold('─── Resultado ─────────────────────────────────────────────\n');
393.             printColoredJson(current);
394.             term('\n');
395.             term.bold('────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────\n');
396. 
397.             if (isDryRun) {
398.                 term.yellow('  (modo dry-run — não será salvo no banco)\n');
399.             }
400. 
401.             term('\n');
402.             term.cyan('Glossário ');
403.             term.gray('(formato: "termo > tradução ; outro > outro" — vazio para confirmar)');
404.             term.cyan(': ');
405. 
406.             const input = await new Promise<string>((resolve) => {
407.                 term.inputField({}, (_, value) => {
408.                     term('\n');
409.                     resolve((value ?? '').trim());
410.                 });
411.             });
412. 
413.             // Empty input = confirm
414.             if (!input) {
415.                 return current;
416.             }
417. 
418.             // Parse and validate
419.             const { entries: newEntries, errors } = parseGlossaryInput(input);
420. 
421.             if (errors.length > 0) {
422.                 for (const err of errors) {
423.                     term.red(`  ✗ ${err}\n`);
424.                 }
425.                 term.yellow('  Por favor, corrija o formato e tente novamente.\n');
426.                 continue;
427.             }
428. 
429.             if (newEntries.length === 0) {
430.                 term.yellow('  Nenhuma entrada reconhecida. Tente novamente.\n');
431.                 continue;
432.             }
433. 
434.             // Save new entries to MongoDB
435.             await saveEntries(newEntries);
436.             term.green(`  ✓ ${newEntries.length} entrada(s) salva(s) no glossário.\n`);
437. 
438.             // Reload and reapply all entries (including newly saved ones)
439.             entries = await loadAllEntries();
440.             current = this.applyGlossaryToOutput(output, entries);
441.         }
442.     }
443. 
444.     // ─── Main loop ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
445.
```

All fixes implemented and tests passing. Here's a summary of what changed:

**`scripts/seed-data/base-provider.ts`**
- **Removed** `truncateStr()` — conflict resolver now shows full values on separate indented lines
- **Added** `printRedJson()` — prints all JSON in `brightRed` for the original EN object
- **`reviewAndConfirmItem`** — now accepts optional `originalItem?` param; when present, prints the EN original in red *before* the translated colored JSON
- **`runInteractiveItem`** — passes `item` as `originalItem` to the review step
- **`applyGlossaryToOutput`** — strips leading/trailing punctuation (`.,;:!?`) from `name` **before** applying the glossary
